province_event = { #Simony
	
	id = dg_catholic.001
	title = dg_catholic.001.t
	desc = dg_catholic.001.d
	picture = catholic_simony
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_year = 1380 }
				NOT = { AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_simony value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #The Western Schism
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_year = 1380
					AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes }
				}
				owner = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = no }
				NOT = { is_year = 1510 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_simony value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #The Printing Press
			limit = {
				owner = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { is_year = 1510 } #Defeat of Conciliarism
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_simony value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #Defeat of Conciliarism
			limit = { is_year = 1510 }
			owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_simony value = 0.1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation } }
				}
				owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 12 } }
					owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 48 } }
					owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = greedy_bishop duration = 2000 }
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 12 } }
			owner = {
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						area = ROOT
						NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
					}
					add_province_modifier = { name = greedy_bishop duration = 2000 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 48 } }
			owner = {
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						region = ROOT
						NOT = { area = ROOT }
						NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
					}
					add_province_modifier = { name = greedy_bishop duration = 2000 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.001.a #The church is for sale
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 1 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = humanism }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				owner = { NOT = { capital_distance = { who = PAP distance = 130 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				owner = { capital_distance = { who = PAP distance = 260 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = renaissance }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = { #Countries that have papal influence are less likely to complain
				owner = {
					num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
						has_province_modifier = catholic_archbishopric
						value = 3
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = ally_of_pope }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = friend_of_pope }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = rival_of_pope }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = simony }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_province_flag = simony_province
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				any_neighbor_province = { has_province_flag = simony_province }
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
					set_province_flag = simony_province
				}
			}
		}
		owner = { set_country_flag = simony }
		PAP = { add_treasury = 5 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					culture = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { num_of_cities = 12 }
						ai = yes
					}
				}
				owner = { set_country_flag = simony }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.001.b #Send a formal protest to Rome
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_cardinals = 1 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_cardinals = 3 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_cardinals = 6 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
					set_province_flag = simony_province
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { DIP = 6 } }
			random = {
				chance = 90
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { DIP = 5 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { DIP = 4 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 60
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { DIP = 3 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 45
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { DIP = 2 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 30
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 15
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					culture_group = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						ai = yes
						NOT = { has_country_flag = simony }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = neighbor_complaint
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						ai = yes
					}
				}
				owner = { set_country_flag = simony }
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_papal_influence = -5
			hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = simony }
			add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = reform_demands_minor }
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Absentee Bishop
	
	id = dg_catholic.002
	title = dg_catholic.002.t
	desc = dg_catholic.002.d
	picture = catholic_corrupt_priest
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_year = 1380 }
				NOT = { AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_absenteeism value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #The Western Schism
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_year = 1380
					AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes }
				}
				owner = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = no }
				NOT = { is_year = 1510 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_absenteeism value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #The Printing Press
			limit = {
				owner = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { is_year = 1510 } #Defeat of Conciliarism
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_absenteeism value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #Defeat of Conciliarism
			limit = { is_year = 1510 }
			owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_absenteeism value = 0.1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation } }
				}
				owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 12 } }
					owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 48 } }
					owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.002.a #Heresy and greed!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				NOT = { owner = { piety = -0.20 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { piety = 0.20 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { piety = 0.60 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 1 } }
				factor = 1.2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = humanism }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = absenteeism }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_province_flag = absentee_bishop
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				any_neighbor_province = { has_province_flag = absentee_bishop }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				owner = { NOT = { capital_distance = { who = PAP distance = 130 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				owner = { capital_distance = { who = PAP distance = 260 } }
			}
			modifier = { #Countries that have papal influence are less likely to complain
				owner = {
					num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
						has_province_modifier = catholic_archbishopric
						value = 3
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = ally_of_pope }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = friend_of_pope }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = rival_of_pope }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope }
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.20 } } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 1000 }
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 12 } }
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							area = ROOT
							NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
							OR = {
								jungle_trigger = yes
								mountains_trigger = yes
								highlands_trigger = yes
								desert_trigger = yes
								has_terrain = marsh
								NOT = { development = 5 }
								steppes_trigger = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
						}
						add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 1000 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 48 } }
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							region = ROOT
							NOT = { area = ROOT }
							NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
							OR = {
								jungle_trigger = yes
								mountains_trigger = yes
								highlands_trigger = yes
								desert_trigger = yes
								has_terrain = marsh
								NOT = { development = 5 }
								steppes_trigger = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
						}
						add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 1000 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { piety = 0.60 } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 8000 }
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 12 } }
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							area = ROOT
							NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
							OR = {
								jungle_trigger = yes
								mountains_trigger = yes
								highlands_trigger = yes
								desert_trigger = yes
								has_terrain = marsh
								NOT = { development = 5 }
								steppes_trigger = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
						}
						add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 8000 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 48 } }
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							region = ROOT
							NOT = { area = ROOT }
							NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
							OR = {
								jungle_trigger = yes
								mountains_trigger = yes
								highlands_trigger = yes
								desert_trigger = yes
								has_terrain = marsh
								NOT = { development = 5 }
								steppes_trigger = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
						}
						add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 8000 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { piety = 0.20 }
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 4000 }
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 12 } }
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							area = ROOT
							NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
							OR = {
								jungle_trigger = yes
								mountains_trigger = yes
								highlands_trigger = yes
								desert_trigger = yes
								has_terrain = marsh
								NOT = { development = 5 }
								steppes_trigger = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
						}
						add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 4000 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 48 } }
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							region = ROOT
							NOT = { area = ROOT }
							NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
							OR = {
								jungle_trigger = yes
								mountains_trigger = yes
								highlands_trigger = yes
								desert_trigger = yes
								has_terrain = marsh
								NOT = { development = 5 }
								steppes_trigger = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
						}
						add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 4000 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { piety = -0.20 }
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 2000 }
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 12 } }
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							area = ROOT
							NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
							OR = {
								jungle_trigger = yes
								mountains_trigger = yes
								highlands_trigger = yes
								desert_trigger = yes
								has_terrain = marsh
								NOT = { development = 5 }
								steppes_trigger = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
						}
						add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 2000 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 48 } }
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							region = ROOT
							NOT = { area = ROOT }
							NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
							OR = {
								jungle_trigger = yes
								mountains_trigger = yes
								highlands_trigger = yes
								desert_trigger = yes
								has_terrain = marsh
								NOT = { development = 5 }
								steppes_trigger = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
							NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
						}
						add_province_modifier = { name = absentee_bishop duration = 2000 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_province_flag = absentee_bishop
			owner = { set_country_flag = absenteeism }
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					culture = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { num_of_cities = 12 }
						ai = yes
					}
				}
				owner = { set_country_flag = absenteeism }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.002.b #Hire a foreign preacher to come to $PROVINCECAPITAL$
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		owner = {
			add_treasury = -5
			set_country_flag = absenteeism
		}
		set_province_flag = absentee_bishop
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					culture_group = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						ai = yes
						NOT = { has_country_flag = absenteeism }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = neighbor_complaint
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						ai = yes
					}
				}
				owner = { set_country_flag = absenteeism }
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #03 - The Bishop's Mistress
	
	id = dg_catholic.003
	title = dg_catholic.003.t
	desc = dg_catholic.003.d
	picture = catholic_papal_nepotism
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_year = 1380 }
				NOT = { AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_clerical_corruption value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #The Western Schism
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_year = 1380
					AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes }
				}
				owner = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = no }
				NOT = { is_year = 1510 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_clerical_corruption value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #The Printing Press
			limit = {
				owner = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { is_year = 1510 } #Defeat of Conciliarism
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_clerical_corruption value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #Defeat of Conciliarism
			limit = { is_year = 1510 }
			owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_clerical_corruption value = 0.1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation } }
				}
				owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 12 } }
					owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 48 } }
					owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				}
			}
			owner = { set_country_flag = papal_nepotism }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.003.a #Look the other way
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 5000 }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.003.b #Get rid of him
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				PAP = { has_country_flag = reformer_pope }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = national_church }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = patronato_real }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					PAP = { has_country_flag = reformer_pope }
					owner = { has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction }
					owner = { has_country_flag = national_church }
					owner = { has_country_flag = patronato_real }
					owner = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				}
			}
			owner = { add_dip_power = -10 }
		}
		else = {
			owner = {
				add_dip_power = -20
				add_papal_influence = -5
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Indulgence Peddler
	
	id = dg_catholic.004
	title = dg_catholic.004.t
	desc = dg_catholic.004.d
	picture = catholic_indulgences
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_year = 1380 }
				NOT = { AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_indulgences value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #The Western Schism
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_year = 1380
					AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes }
				}
				owner = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = no }
				NOT = { is_year = 1510 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_indulgences value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #The Printing Press
			limit = {
				owner = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { is_year = 1510 } #Defeat of Conciliarism
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_indulgences value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #Defeat of Conciliarism
			limit = { is_year = 1510 }
			owner = { add_reform_desire = 0.001 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_indulgences value = 0.1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation } }
				}
				owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 12 } }
					owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 48 } }
					owner = { change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = indulgence_peddler duration = 400 }
		set_province_flag = indulgence_peddler
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 12 } }
			owner = {
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						area = ROOT
						NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
					}
					add_province_modifier = { name = indulgence_peddler duration = 400 }
					set_province_flag = indulgence_peddler
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 48 } }
			owner = {
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						region = ROOT
						NOT = { area = ROOT }
						NOT = { province_id = ROOT }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
					}
					add_province_modifier = { name = indulgence_peddler duration = 400 }
					set_province_flag = indulgence_peddler
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.004.a #Purchase absolution for the $MONARCH$
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owner = { have_religious_scandal = yes }
				has_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				owner = { years_of_income = 0.5 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { years_of_income = 1 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { years_of_income = 2 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { years_of_income = 0.25 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { years_of_income = 0.10 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 1 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 2 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { is_bankrupt = yes }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { piety = 0.60 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { piety = 0.20 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.20 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.60 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		owner = {
			dg_add_legitimacy = yes
			if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 50 }
				add_treasury = -50
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
				add_years_of_income = -0.08
			}
			else = {
				add_treasury = -5
			}
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				religious_scandal_country_strong = {
					remove_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
				}
				religious_scandal_country = {
					remove_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
				}
				religious_scandal_country_weak = {
					remove_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
				}
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }
		}
		remove_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province
		hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = indulgences_sold value = 1 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.004.b #Allow this practice
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.004.c #Condemn the practice
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = indulgences_condemned }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_province_flag = indulgence_peddler
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 2 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 4 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 6 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 8 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { check_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 10 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		owner = {
			hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = indulgences_condemned }
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = disobeyed_religious_leader }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { DIP = 6 } }
			random = { chance = 90 remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { DIP = 5 }
				}
			random = { chance = 75 remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { DIP = 4 }
			}
			random = { chance = 60 remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { DIP = 3 }
			}
			random = { chance = 45 remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { DIP = 2 }
			}
			random = { chance = 30 remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
		}
		else = {
			random = { chance = 15 remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					culture_group = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						ai = yes
						NOT = { has_country_flag = indulgences_condemned }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = neighbor_complaint
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						ai = yes
					}
				}
				owner = { set_country_flag = indulgences_condemned }
			}
		}
	}
}

		if = { #Defeat of Conciliarism
			limit = { is_year = 1510 religion = catholic }
			add_reform_desire = 0.001
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_ecclesiastical_courts value = 0.1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation }
				}
				change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.005.a #Submit to the authority of the church
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { religion = catholic }
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_owner_religion = yes controlled_by = ROOT }
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 1 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -1
			add_country_modifier = { name = anticlericalism duration = 100 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -2
			add_country_modifier = { name = anticlericalism duration = 200 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -3
			add_country_modifier = { name = anticlericalism duration = 400 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = -4
			add_country_modifier = { name = anticlericalism duration = 800 }
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -5
			add_country_modifier = { name = anticlericalism duration = 1600 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.005.b #Sentence them under secular law
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		if = {
			limit = { religion = catholic }
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = disobeyed_religious_leader }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 400 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 400 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 400 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #06 - Popular Piety
	
	id = dg_catholic.006
	title = dg_catholic.006.t
	desc = dg_catholic.006.d
	picture = all_pilgrims #TEMP
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation }
				}
				change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.006.a #Embrace popular piety
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = renaissance
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = humanism
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cardinals = 1
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cardinals = 3
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cardinals = 5
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_year = 1380 }
				NOT = { AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_reform_desire = 0.001
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_popular_piety value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { #The Western Schism
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_year = 1380
					AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes }
				}
				has_casual_literacy_trigger = no
				NOT = { is_year = 1510 }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				add_reform_desire = 0.001
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_popular_piety value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { #The Printing Press
			limit = {
				has_casual_literacy_trigger = yes
				NOT = { is_year = 1510 } #Defeat of Conciliarism
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				add_reform_desire = 0.001
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_popular_piety value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { #Defeat of Conciliarism
			limit = { is_year = 1510 }
			add_reform_desire = 0.001
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_popular_piety value = 0.1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = catholic_popular_piety
		add_piety = 0.10
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.006.b #Embrace anticlericalism
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		add_papal_influence = -10
		set_country_flag = catholic_anticlericalism
		add_piety = -0.10
	}
}

country_event = { #Birth of the Conciliar Movement
	
	id = dg_catholic.007
	title = dg_catholic.007.t
	desc = dg_catholic.007.d
	picture = catholic_church_council
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		exists = AVI
		AVI = { papal_trigger = yes }
		OR = {
			advisor = theologian
			is_emperor = yes
		}
		PAP = { NOT = { has_country_flag = conciliar_movement } }
		PAP = { NOT = { has_country_flag = papal_absolutism } }
		is_colonial_nation = no
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 25 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { PAP = { set_country_flag = conciliar_movement } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_religion_enabled = hussite }
				NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant }
				NOT = { is_religion_enabled = reformed }
			}
			add_reform_desire = 0.01
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_conciliarism value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_religion_enabled = hussite
				NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant }
				NOT = { is_religion_enabled = reformed }
			}
			add_reform_desire = 0.02
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_conciliarism value = 2 } }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_religion_enabled = protestant
				NOT = { is_religion_enabled = reformed }
			}
			add_reform_desire = 0.03
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_conciliarism value = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_religion_enabled = reformed }
			add_reform_desire = 0.04
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_conciliarism value = 4 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.007.a #Support the movement
		trigger = { papal_trigger = no }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				is_emperor = yes
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cardinals = 3
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cardinals = 6
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cardinals = 9
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { capital_distance = { who = ROOT distance = 260 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { capital_distance = { who = ROOT distance = 390 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = conciliarism_supported
		add_papal_influence = -5
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = disobeyed_religious_leader }
		dg_add_legitimacy = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { advisor = theologian } }
			define_advisor = { religion = catholic type = theologian discount = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_emperor = yes }
			add_prestige = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.007.b #Ignore the movement
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 10
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 20
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = conciliarism_ignored
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_controversy duration = 500 }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.007.c #Actively suppress the movement
		trigger = {
			is_emperor = no
			OR = {
				NOT = { exists = AVI }
				AVI = { papal_trigger = no }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				papal_trigger = yes
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				advisor = theologian
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 10
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 20
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 30
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = excommunicated
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = great_matter
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = papal_interference
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = conciliarism_suppressed
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }
		add_papal_influence = 5
		if = {
			limit = { advisor = theologian }
			remove_advisor = theologian
			add_patriarch_authority = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 500 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 500 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Catholic Maintenance event
	
	id = dg_catholic.011
	title = ai_only.t
	desc = ai_only.d
	picture = ai_only
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = minority_timer_catholic }
		OR = {
			piety = -0.60
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 25
		
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = minority_timer_catholic duration = 300 hidden = yes }
		set_country_flag = catholic_event
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ai_only.a
		if = { #Preferred events (checked first if conditions met)
			limit = {
				papal_trigger = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = national_church }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = patronato_real }
			}
			if = { #Popular Piety
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = catholic_event
					NOT = { has_country_flag = catholic_popular_piety }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = catholic_anticlericalism }
					NOT = { has_global_flag = counter_reformation }
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = absenteeism
						has_country_flag = simony
						has_country_flag = indulgences_condemned
						has_country_flag = royal_scandal
						has_country_flag = canonical_court_scandal
						AVI = { papal_trigger = yes num_of_cities = 1 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						has_country_flag = absenteeism
					}
					random = {
						chance = 6
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						country_event = { id = dg_catholic.006 } #Popular Piety
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						has_country_flag = simony
					}
					random = {
						chance = 6
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						country_event = { id = dg_catholic.006 } #Popular Piety
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						has_country_flag = indulgences_condemned
					}
					random = {
						chance = 6
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						country_event = { id = dg_catholic.006 } #Popular Piety
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						has_country_flag = royal_scandal
					}
					random = {
						chance = 6
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						country_event = { id = dg_catholic.006 } #Popular Piety
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						has_country_flag = canonical_court_scandal
					}
					random = {
						chance = 6
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						country_event = { id = dg_catholic.006 } #Popular Piety
					}
				}
			}
			if = { #Indulgences
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = catholic_event
					PAP = { has_country_flag = indulgences_permitted }
					PAP = { NOT = { has_country_flag = indulgences_banned } }
					NOT = { government = theocracy }
					any_owned_province = {
						continent = europe
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = effective_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						OR = {
							has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
							has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
							has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
							has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
							has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
							has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
							has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
							has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
						}
					}
					random = {
						chance = 20
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									ai = yes
									has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial

															NOT = { has_province_flag = monastic_order }
														}

													}
												}

													limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 72 } }

														limit = {
															owned_by = ROOT
															NOT = { area = PREV }

																NOT = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 18 } } #Rooted out heresy

															NOT = { has_province_modifier = dominican_order }
															NOT = { has_province_modifier = cistercian_order }
															NOT = { has_province_modifier = franciscan_order }

														clr_province_flag = monastic_order
													}

											}

###############
# Monasticism #

province_event = { #Monasticism
	
	id = dg_catholic.013
	title = dg_catholic.013.t
	desc = dg_catholic.013.d
	picture = catholic_monks
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_province_flag = augustinian_order
			set_province_flag = dominican_order
			set_province_flag = cistercian_order
			set_province_flag = franciscan_order
			set_province_flag = jesuit_order
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 72 } }
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						area = ROOT
						OR = {
							#has_terrain = farmlands #Involved in agriculture
							trade_goods = wine
							trade_goods = wool
							farming_province_trigger = yes
							has_province_modifier = catholic_pilgrimage
						}
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = augustinian_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = dominican_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = cistercian_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = franciscan_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = jesuit_order }
						NOT = { has_province_flag = augustinian_order }
					}
					set_province_flag = augustinian_order
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						NOT = { area = ROOT }

							has_province_modifier = catholic_archbishopric
							has_province_modifier = catholic_prelate
						}
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = augustinian_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = dominican_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = cistercian_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = franciscan_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = jesuit_order }
						NOT = { has_province_flag = jesuit_order }
					}
					set_province_flag = jesuit_order
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.013.a #Augustinians
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {

				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		owner = {

				limit = { has_province_flag = augustinian_order }
				add_province_modifier = { name = augustinian_order duration = 10000 }
				remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
				clr_province_flag = augustinian_order
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					clr_province_flag = augustinian_order
					clr_province_flag = dominican_order
					clr_province_flag = cistercian_order
					clr_province_flag = franciscan_order
					clr_province_flag = jesuit_order
				}
			}
		}
	}

province_event = { #Augustinian Monks
	
	id = dg_catholic.015
	title = dg_catholic.015.t

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_province_flag = monastic_order

				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 72 } }
				random_province = {
					limit = {

						area = PREV
						OR = {

						NOT = { has_province_modifier = cistercian_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = franciscan_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = jesuit_order }
						NOT = { has_province_flag = monastic_order }
					}
					set_province_flag = monastic_order
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						NOT = { area = PREV }

							#has_terrain = farmlands #Involved in agriculture

country_event = { #215 - Agricultural Innovation (Augustinian, Cistercian)
	
	id = dg_catholic.215
	title = dg_catholic.215.t
	desc = dg_catholic.215.d
	picture = catholic_monastic_town
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.215.a #Force the peasants to adopt these new techniques
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 2
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				war_exhaustion = 2
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				war_exhaustion = 4
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				war_exhaustion = 6
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				war_exhaustion = 8
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				war_exhaustion = 10
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_war_exhaustion = 2
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = augustinian_order
					has_province_modifier = cistercian_order
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = new_agricultural_techniques }
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = new_agricultural_techniques duration = 5000 }
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 2 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.215.b #Give them incentives to adopt them
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				num_of_loans = 1
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_loans = 2
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_bankrupt = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				treasury = 100
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				treasury = 200
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				treasury = 400
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				treasury = 800
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = augustinian_order
						has_province_modifier = cistercian_order
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = new_agricultural_techniques }
					value = 8
				}
			}
			add_treasury = -50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = augustinian_order
						has_province_modifier = cistercian_order
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = new_agricultural_techniques }
					value = 4
				}
			}
			add_treasury = -25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = augustinian_order
						has_province_modifier = cistercian_order
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = new_agricultural_techniques }
					value = 2
				}
			}
			add_treasury = -10
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = -5
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = augustinian_order
					has_province_modifier = cistercian_order
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = new_agricultural_techniques }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				add_province_modifier = { name = new_agricultural_techniques duration = 5000 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.215.c #Leave them alone
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		add_prestige = -1
	}
}

				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						area = ROOT
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 20 } } #Rooted out heresy
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = augustinian_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = dominican_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = cistercian_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = franciscan_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = jesuit_order }
						NOT = { has_province_flag = monastic_order }
					}
					set_province_flag = monastic_order
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT

						region = ROOT
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 20 } } #Rooted out heresy

						NOT = { has_province_flag = monastic_order }
					}
					set_province_flag = monastic_order
				}
			}

						NOT = { has_province_modifier = franciscan_order }
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = jesuit_order }
						NOT = { has_province_flag = monastic_order }

	}

				clr_province_flag = monastic_order
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #216 - Book Burning (Dominican)
	
	id = dg_catholic.216
	title = dg_catholic.216.t
	desc = dg_catholic.216.d
	picture = book_burning
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.216.a #Encourage the purge
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				government = theocracy
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = book_burning duration = 4000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = book_burning duration = 3200 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = book_burning duration = 2400 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = book_burning duration = 1600 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = book_burning duration = 800 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.216.b #Discourage the purge
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { ADM = 2 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { ADM = 3 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				ADM = 5
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				ADM = 6
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		add_adm_power = -25
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = book_burning duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = book_burning duration = 800 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = book_burning duration = 600 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = book_burning duration = 400 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = book_burning duration = 200 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.216.c #Ban the purge
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 2000 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 2000 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Monastic protests
	
	id = dg_catholic.217
	title = dg_catholic.217.t
	desc = dg_catholic.217.d
	picture = all_church_resistance
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.217.a #Promise to improve the lot of the poor
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_province = {
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = dominican_order
							has_province_modifier = franciscan_order
							has_province_modifier = jesuit_order
						}
						unrest = 2
					}
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		add_adm_power = -25
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = dominican_order
					has_province_modifier = franciscan_order
					has_province_modifier = jesuit_order
				}
			}
			add_local_autonomy = 5
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = -2 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.217.b #Ignore the protests
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = dominican_order
					has_province_modifier = franciscan_order
					has_province_modifier = jesuit_order
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 1 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_1
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core = owner } }
				add_nationalism = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.217.c #Arrest the monks
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 2000 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 2000 }
		}
	}

					any_owned_province = {
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = cistercian_order
							has_province_modifier = franciscan_order
						}
						local_autonomy = 5
					}
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {

					any_owned_province = {

						}

					}

		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = cistercian_order
					has_province_modifier = franciscan_order
				}
			}
			add_local_autonomy = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.218.b #Impose one rule upon them
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.40
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 500 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 500 }
		}
	}

	# Appeal to the pope to decide
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.218.c

		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = PAP }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}

		add_prestige = -5
	}
}

country_event = { #219 - Monks preach against heresy (Jesuit, Dominican, Augustinian)
	
	id = dg_catholic.219
	title = dg_catholic.219.t
	desc = dg_catholic.219.d
	picture = catholic_monks_preaching
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.219.a #Encourage them
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 4000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 3200 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 2400 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 1600 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 800 }
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = jesuit_order
					has_province_modifier = dominican_order
					has_province_modifier = augustinian_order
				}
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 18 } }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { which = added_unrest value = 2 }
				add_base_unrest = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
			if = {
				limit = { nationalism = 1 }
				add_nationalism = 2
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				custom_tooltip = catholic_10
				hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = converted_heretics value = 2 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { religion_group = ROOT } }
				hidden_effect = { random = { chance = 25 change_variable = { which = converted_heathens value = 2 } } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion_group = pagan
						religion_group = european_pagan
						religion_group = new_world_pagan
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = converted_heathens value = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.219.b #Discourage them
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 500 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 500 }
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Canonization of a Saint
	
	id = dg_catholic.021
	title = dg_catholic.021.t
	desc = dg_catholic.021.d
	picture = catholic_canonization
	
	trigger = {
		PAP = { NOT = { has_country_flag = canonization } } #Once per pope
		check_variable = { which = catholic value = 4 }
		owner = { religion = catholic }
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = catholic_pilgrimage }
		NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = catholic_pilgrimage } }
		NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = catholic_pilgrimage } } }
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope } #The pope plays favorites
			NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hiding_luther }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = sheltered_luther }
			papal_trigger = no
			not_have_religious_scandal = yes
			piety = -0.60
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				has_country_flag = religious_news_major
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 250
		
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = sainthood_candidate }
			factor = 0.25
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { religion = catholic }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = friend_of_pope }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = ally_of_pope }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = rival_of_pope }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = national_saint }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.20 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { piety = 0.20 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { piety = 0.60 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { num_of_cities = 3 } }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 5 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 10 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 20 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 40 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 80 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 160 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				set_country_flag = national_saint
				clr_country_flag = sainthood_candidate
			}
			PAP = { set_country_flag = canonization }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.021.a #Celebrate this miracle
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				owner = { piety = 0.20 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { piety = 0.60 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.20 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.60 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { stability = -2 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { stability = -1 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_papal_influence = 4
				add_prestige = 16
				add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_great }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { stability = 0 }
					}
					add_stability_1 = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_papal_influence = 3
				add_prestige = 12
				add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_great }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { stability = -1 }
					}
					add_stability_1 = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_papal_influence = 2
				add_prestige = 8
				add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_great }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { stability = -2 }
					}
					add_stability_1 = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_papal_influence = 1
				add_prestige = 4
				add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_good }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.021.b #Turn $PROVINCENAME$ into a center of pilgrimage
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				owner = { stability = 1 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { stability = 2 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { stability = 3 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 1 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 2 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { is_bankrupt = yes }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { treasury = 10 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { treasury = 25 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = catholic_pilgrimage duration = -1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				temple_trigger = no
				cathedral_trigger = no
				num_free_building_slots = 1
			}
			add_building = temple
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Candidate for sainthood
	
	id = dg_catholic.022
	title = dg_catholic.022.t
	desc = dg_catholic.022.d
	picture = catholic_canonization
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		is_at_war = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = sainthood_candidate }
		papal_trigger = no
		piety = -0.60
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_country_flag = religious_news_major
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 166
		
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.022.a #Celebrate their life
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = 4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = 3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = 2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.022.b #Send a mission to Rome to plead their case
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = friend_of_pope
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = ally_of_pope
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = national_saint
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		add_papal_influence = -5
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = sainthood_candidate }
		custom_tooltip = sainthood_candidate_explained
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = 4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = 3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = 2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = 1
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #The First Estate
	
	id = dg_catholic.023
	title = dg_catholic.023.t
	desc = dg_catholic.023.d
	picture = catholic_bishop
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		PAP = { NOT = { has_country_flag = peasant_success } } #Once per pope
		OR = {
			owner = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } }
		}
		owner = {
			religion = catholic
			piety = -0.60
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 250
		
		modifier = {
			NOT = { owner = { piety = -0.20 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { piety = 0.20 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { piety = 0.60 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = national_church }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { num_of_cities = 3 } }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 5 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 10 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 20 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 40 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 80 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 160 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { hidden_effect = { PAP = { set_country_flag = peasant_success } } }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.023.a #Let the peasants have their hero
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { piety = 0.60 } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = peasant_success_story duration = 1600 }
			owner = { add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_good } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { owner = { piety = 0.20 } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = peasant_success_story duration = 800 }
			owner = { add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_good } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { owner = { piety = -0.20 } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = peasant_success_story duration = 400 }
			owner = { add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_good } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { owner = { piety = -0.60 } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = peasant_success_story duration = 200 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.023.b #Hold him up as a model
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				owner = { piety = 0.60 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { piety = 0.20 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.20 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 1 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 2 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { is_bankrupt = yes }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { treasury = 5 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { treasury = 10 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { NOT = { treasury = 25 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		owner = { add_treasury = -5 }
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { piety = 0.60 } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = peasant_success_story duration = 3200 }
			owner = { add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_great } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { owner = { piety = 0.20 } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = peasant_success_story duration = 1600 }
			owner = { add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_great } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { owner = { piety = -0.20 } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = peasant_success_story duration = 800 }
			owner = { add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_great } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { owner = { piety = -0.60 } }
			add_province_modifier = { name = peasant_success_story duration = 400 }
			owner = { add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_good } }
		}
	}
