province_event = { #Bishop of $PROVINCENAME$
	
	id = dg_catholic.024
	title = dg_catholic.024.t
	desc = dg_catholic.024.d
	picture = catholic_bishop
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_province_flag = effective_bishop
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 72 } }
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						area = ROOT
						NOT = { has_province_flag = effective_bishop }
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						NOT = { area = ROOT }
						region = ROOT
						NOT = { has_province_flag = effective_bishop }
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						NOT = { area = ROOT }
						region = ROOT
						NOT = { has_province_flag = effective_bishop }
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 24 } }
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						area = ROOT
						NOT = { has_province_flag = effective_bishop }
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						NOT = { area = ROOT }
						region = ROOT
						NOT = { has_province_flag = effective_bishop }
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 8 } }
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						area = ROOT
						NOT = { has_province_flag = effective_bishop }
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.024.a #Promote peace and order
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		owner = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = effective_bishop }
				add_province_modifier = { name = effective_bishop duration = 8000 }
				remove_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province
				remove_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
				remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
				remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
				clr_province_flag = effective_bishop
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.024.b #Take an interest in his career
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				owner = { num_of_loans = 1 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { is_bankrupt = yes }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					any_owned_province = {
						any_neighbor_province = { has_province_flag = effective_bishop }
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
							has_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 3
			}
		}
		owner = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_province_flag = effective_bishop
						any_neighbor_province = { has_province_flag = effective_bishop }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = effective_bishop }
					add_province_modifier = { name = effective_bishop duration = 8000 }
				}
				remove_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province
				remove_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
				remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
				remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
				clr_province_flag = effective_bishop
			}
			if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 100 }
				add_treasury = -50
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 10 }
				add_years_of_income = -0.04
			}
			else = {
				add_treasury = -5
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = { owner = { define_advisor = { religion = catholic culture = ROOT type = theologian discount = yes } } }
			50 = { owner = { define_advisor = { religion = catholic culture = ROOT type = inquisitor discount = yes } } }
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #$PROVINCECAPITAL$ is elevated to an archbishopric
	
	id = dg_catholic.025
	title = dg_catholic.025.t
	desc = dg_catholic.025.d
	picture = catholic_bishop
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { NOT = { tag = PAP } }
		OR = {
			is_capital = yes
			has_province_modifier = effective_bishop
		}
		urban_province_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			continent = europe
			rich_province_trigger = yes
		}
		owner = { religion = catholic }
		OR = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 10 }
			AND = {
				superregion = italy_superregion
				has_owner_culture = yes
			}
		}
		owner = {
			NOT = { war_with = PAP }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hiding_luther }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = sheltered_luther }
			piety = -0.60
			patriarch_authority = 0.40
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent }
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				has_country_flag = religious_news_major
			}
		}
		OR = {
			is_capital = yes
			AND = {
				superregion = italy_superregion
				has_owner_culture = yes
				rich_province_trigger = yes
			}
			NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { any_neighbor_province = { has_province_flag = catholic_archbishopric } } }
		}
		any_neighbor_province = { owner = { religion = catholic } } #No one province islands
		NOT = { has_province_flag = catholic_archbishopric }
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop }
		is_core = owner
		controlled_by = owner
		has_siege = no
		has_global_flag = living_pope
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 83
		
		modifier = {
			is_capital = yes
			has_province_modifier = effective_bishop
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			is_in_capital_area = no
			factor = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { piety = 0.60 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { piety = 0.20 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.20 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { piety = -0.60 } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cardinals = 3 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cardinals = 6 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cardinals = 9 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { religion = catholic }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = catholic_prelate
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.025.a #An honor indeed
		set_province_flag = catholic_archbishopric
		add_province_modifier = { name = catholic_archbishopric duration = -1 }
		#if = {
		#	limit = {
		#		temple_trigger = yes
		#		cathedral_trigger = no
		#		num_free_building_slots = 1
		#		}
		#	add_building = great_temple
		#	remove_building = temple
		#	}
		if = {
			limit = {
				temple_trigger = no
				cathedral_trigger = no
				num_free_building_slots = 1
			}
			add_building = temple
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { religion = catholic } }
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -4 }
				change_variable = { which = catholic value = 4 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = 4
				add_papal_influence = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = 3
				add_papal_influence = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = 2
				add_papal_influence = 4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = 1
				add_papal_influence = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Resolving a Grievance
	
	id = dg_catholic.026
	title = dg_catholic.026.t
	desc = dg_catholic.026.d
	picture = catholic_papal_legate
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		OR = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.60
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } }
		}
		NOT = { any_neighbor_country = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party } }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
		exists = PAP
		papal_trigger = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction }
		any_neighbor_country = {
			religion = catholic
			NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
			ai = yes
			NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
			NOT = { vassal_of = ROOT }
			NOT = { overlord_of = ROOT }
			NOT = { junior_union_with = ROOT }
			NOT = { senior_union_with = ROOT }
			NOT = { stability = 2 }
			NOT = { has_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 } }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction }
			OR = {
				overextension_percentage = 0.25
				num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
				truce_with = ROOT
				culture_group = ROOT
				trade_embargo_by = ROOT
				is_rival = ROOT
			}
		}
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_country_flag = religious_news_major
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 416
		
		modifier = {
			NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } } }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			exists = AVI
			AVI = { papal_trigger = yes }
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
				ai = yes
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { vassal_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { overlord_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { junior_union_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { senior_union_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { stability = 2 }
				NOT = { has_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 } }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction }
				OR = {
					overextension_percentage = 0.25
					num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
					truce_with = ROOT
					culture_group = ROOT
					trade_embargo_by = ROOT
					is_rival = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = aggrieved_party
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						OR = {
							truce_with = ROOT
							overextension_percentage = 0.25
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = grievance_military
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
					set_country_flag = grievance_military
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier }
						any_neighbor_country = {
							has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
							OR = {
								any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier }
								trade_embargo_by = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = grievance_trade
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
					set_country_flag = grievance_trade
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = grievance_military }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = grievance_trade }
				}
				set_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
					set_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.026.a #Try to resolve the situation ourselves
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_military }
			add_mil_power = -100 # add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_military_funding duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_trade }
			add_country_modifier = { name = minor_trade_crisis duration = 2000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic }
			if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 50 }
				add_treasury = -100
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
					add_treasury = 100
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 25 }
				add_treasury = -50
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
					add_treasury = 50
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 10 }
				add_treasury = -25
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
					add_treasury = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
				add_treasury = -10
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
					add_treasury = 10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 2 }
				add_treasury = -5
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
					add_treasury = 5
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_treasury = -2
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
					add_treasury = 2
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { DIP = 5 }
			random_list = {
				100 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { DIP = 4 }
			random_list = {
				90 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
				10 = { add_prestige = -5 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { DIP = 3 }
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
				30 = { add_prestige = -5 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { DIP = 2 }
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
				50 = { add_prestige = -5 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				30 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
				70 = { add_prestige = -5 }
			}
		}
		#Cleanup
		hidden_effect = {
			random_neighbor_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
				clr_country_flag = aggrieved_party
				clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
				clr_country_flag = grievance_military
				clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
			}
			clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			clr_country_flag = grievance_military
			clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.026.b #Rattle our sabres until they back down
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
					truce_with = ROOT
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
					NOT = { army_size = ROOT }
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 2
				any_neighbor_country = {
					has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
					NOT = { num_of_cities = 2 }
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 5
				any_neighbor_country = {
					has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
					NOT = { num_of_cities = 3 }
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 10
				any_neighbor_country = {
					has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
					NOT = { num_of_cities = 5 }
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 20
				any_neighbor_country = {
					has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
					NOT = { num_of_cities = 10 }
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 40
				any_neighbor_country = {
					has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
					NOT = { num_of_cities = 20 }
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						NOT = { army_size = ROOT }
					}
				}
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities = 2
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						NOT = { num_of_cities = 2 }
					}
				}
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities = 5
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						NOT = { num_of_cities = 3 }
					}
				}
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities = 10
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						NOT = { num_of_cities = 5 }
					}
				}
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities = 20
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						NOT = { num_of_cities = 10 }
					}
				}
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities = 40
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						NOT = { num_of_cities = 20 }
					}
				}
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						is_at_war = yes
					}
				}
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						war_exhaustion = 10
					}
				}
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.20 }
					}
				}
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { MIL = 5 }
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { manpower_percentage = 0.80 }
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { war_exhaustion = 1 } }
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_at_war = yes }
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = -1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.20 } }
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = -1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { war_exhaustion = 10 }
				change_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 6 } }
			random_list = {
				100 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 5 }
			}
			random_list = {
				90 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
				10 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_casus_belli = { type = cb_insult months = 12 target = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 4 }
			}
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
				30 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_casus_belli = { type = cb_insult months = 12 target = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 3 }
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
				50 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_casus_belli = { type = cb_insult months = 12 target = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 2 }
			}
			random_list = {
				30 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
				70 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_casus_belli = { type = cb_insult months = 12 target = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
					}
				}
				90 = {
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_casus_belli = { type = cb_insult months = 12 target = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#Cleanup
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = military_threat_level value = 0 }
			random_neighbor_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
				clr_country_flag = aggrieved_party
				clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
				clr_country_flag = grievance_military
				clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
			}
			clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			clr_country_flag = grievance_military
			clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.026.c #Ask the pope to arbitrate the issue
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				is_papal_controller = yes
				factor = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = friend_of_pope
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = ally_of_pope
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { has_country_flag = corrupt_pope }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { has_country_flag = reformer_pope }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		add_papal_influence = -5
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
			country_event = { id = dg_pope.014 days = 90 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.026.e #Send generous gifts to ensure the pope sees things our way
		trigger = { is_papal_controller = no }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = friend_of_pope
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = ally_of_pope
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_papal_controller = yes
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { has_country_flag = corrupt_pope }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { has_country_flag = reformer_pope }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_loans = 1
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { treasury = 10 }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = papal_bribes_explained
		if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 50 }
			add_treasury = -50
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 50 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 25 }
			add_treasury = -25
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 25 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 10 }
			add_treasury = -10
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 10 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
			add_treasury = -5
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 5 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 2 }
			add_treasury = -2
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 2 } }
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = -1
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 1 } }
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
			country_event = { id = dg_pope.014 days = 90 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The pope rules in our favor
	
	id = dg_catholic.027
	title = dg_catholic.027.t
	desc = dg_catholic.027.d
	picture = catholic_trial
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		dg_add_legitimacy = yes
		add_prestige = 5
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.027.a #Be lenient in victory
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					papal_trigger = yes
					is_papal_controller = yes
				}
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = papacy_great }
		}
		random_neighbor_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
			set_country_flag = lenient_ruling
			remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance }
			add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_bad }
			country_event = { id = dg_catholic.028 days = 30 }
		}
		#Cleanup
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			clr_country_flag = grievance_military
			clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.027.b #Demand justice be served
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					papal_trigger = yes
					is_papal_controller = yes
				}
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = papacy_great }
		}
		random_neighbor_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
			add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_bad }
			country_event = { id = dg_catholic.028 days = 30 }
		}
		#Cleanup
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			clr_country_flag = grievance_military
			clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The pope rules against us
	
	id = dg_catholic.028
	title = dg_catholic.028.t
	desc = dg_catholic.028.d
	picture = catholic_trial
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
			hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
			FROM = { set_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.028.a #Submit gracefully in defeat
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = grievance_military
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = lenient_ruling
				}
				add_mil_power = -100 # add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_military_funding duration = 1000 }
			}
			else = {
				add_mil_power = -200 # add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_military_funding duration = 2000 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = grievance_trade
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = lenient_ruling
				}
				add_country_modifier = { name = minor_trade_crisis duration = 2000 }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = minor_trade_crisis duration = 4000 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = lenient_ruling
				}
				if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 50 }
					add_treasury = -100
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 100
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 25 }
					add_treasury = -50
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 50
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 10 }
					add_treasury = -25
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 25
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
					add_treasury = -10
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 10
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 2 }
					add_treasury = -5
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 5
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_treasury = -2
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 50 }
					add_treasury = -200
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 200
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 25 }
					add_treasury = -100
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 100
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 10 }
					add_treasury = -50
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 50
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
					add_treasury = -25
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 25
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 2 }
					add_treasury = -10
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
						add_treasury = 10
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_treasury = -2
					random_neighbor_country = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
							add_treasury = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_prestige = -5
		#Cleanup
		hidden_effect = {
			random_neighbor_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
				clr_country_flag = aggrieved_party
				clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
				clr_country_flag = grievance_military
				clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
			}
			set_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			clr_country_flag = grievance_military
			clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.028.b #Reject this arbitrary ruling
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		dg_reduce_legitimacy = yes
		random_neighbor_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
			add_casus_belli = { type = cb_insult months = 12 target = ROOT }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#Cleanup
			random_neighbor_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = aggrieved_party }
				clr_country_flag = aggrieved_party
				clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
				clr_country_flag = grievance_military
				clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
			}
			set_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			clr_country_flag = grievance_military
			clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The pope brokers a compromise
	
	id = dg_catholic.029
	title = dg_catholic.029.t
	desc = dg_catholic.029.d
	picture = catholic_papal_legate
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.029.a #Make unpopular changes to heal the rift
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_military }
			add_mil_power = -50 # add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_military_funding duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_trade }
			add_country_modifier = { name = minor_trade_crisis duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			}
			if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 50 }
				add_treasury = -50
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_compromise }
					add_treasury = 50
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 25 }
				add_treasury = -25
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_compromise }
					add_treasury = 25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 10 }
				add_treasury = -10
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_compromise }
					add_treasury = 10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
				add_treasury = -5
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_compromise }
					add_treasury = 5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { monthly_income = 2 }
				add_treasury = -2
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_compromise }
					add_treasury = 2
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_treasury = -1
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_compromise }
					add_treasury = 1
				}
			}
		}
		add_prestige = -5
		dg_add_legitimacy = yes
		add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_good }
		random_neighbor_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_compromise }
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = grievance_resolved }
			hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = grievance_compromise }
		}
		#Cleanup
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = aggrieved_party
			set_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			clr_country_flag = grievance_military
			clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.029.b #Make a token change to mollify the church
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_prestige = -5
		#Cleanup
		hidden_effect = {
			random_neighbor_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = grievance_compromise }
				clr_country_flag = grievance_compromise
			}
			clr_country_flag = aggrieved_party
			set_variable = { which = arbitration_bribe value = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			clr_country_flag = grievance_military
			clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #30 - Our Lady of [Lourdes]
	
	id = dg_catholic.030
	title = dg_catholic.030.t
	desc = dg_catholic.030.d
	picture = orthodox_icon
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

			if = {
				limit = { religion = catholic }

					limit = { piety = 0.60 }

				else_if = {
					limit = { piety = -0.20 }

				}
				else = {
					ROOT = { add_province_modifier = { name = catholic_pilgrimage duration = 1500 } }

		}
	}

						advisor = theologian

					}
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_papal_influence = 5
			dg_add_legitimacy = yes
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				ROOT = { add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 1600 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				ROOT = { add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 1200 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				ROOT = { add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 800 } }
			}
			else = {
				ROOT = { add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 400 } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.030.c #Charge believers to witness it
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
				owner = {
					NOT = { piety = -0.20 }

				}

			}

				limit = { piety = 0.20 }

					limit = { monthly_income = 60 }
					add_treasury = 90
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 6 }
					add_years_of_income = 0.12
				}

					add_treasury = 9
				}
				if = {
					limit = { religion = catholic }
					ROOT = { add_province_modifier = { name = catholic_pilgrimage duration = 4500 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { religion = coptic }

				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 6 }

				}

			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 60 }
					add_treasury = 30
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { monthly_income = 6 }
					add_years_of_income = 0.04

					ROOT = { add_province_modifier = { name = catholic_pilgrimage duration = 1500 } }

				}

		}

province_event = { #301 - The Glory of God (relics recovered)
	
	id = dg_catholic.301
	title = dg_catholic.301.t
	desc = dg_catholic.301.d
	picture = catholic_reliquary_saffron
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		check_variable = { which = christian_relics value = 1 }
		NOT = { controlled_by = owner }
		controller = {
			religion_group = christian
			NOT = { religion = reformed }
			NOT = { religion = protestant }
			piety = -0.60
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 25
		
		modifier = {
			controller = { piety = 0.60 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			controller = { piety = 0.20 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			controller = { NOT = { piety = -0.20 } }
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ai_only.a
		controller = { country_event = { id = dg_catholic.302 } }
		remove_province_modifier = catholic_pilgrimage
		remove_province_modifier = coptic_pilgrimage
		remove_province_modifier = pilgrimage_route
		if = {
			limit = { religion_group = christian }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = christian_relics value = 5 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_unrest duration = 500 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 4 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_unrest duration = 400 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 3 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_unrest duration = 300 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 2 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_unrest duration = 200 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 1 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_unrest duration = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	
	id = dg_catholic.302
	title = dg_catholic.301.t

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { check_variable = { which = christian_relics value = 5 } } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = christian_relics }
				custom_tooltip = christian_relics_5a
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = christian_relics_5b
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 4 } } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = christian_relics }
				custom_tooltip = christian_relics_4a
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = christian_relics_4b
			}
		}
		else_if = {

				custom_tooltip = christian_relics_3a
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = christian_relics_3b
			}
		}

				custom_tooltip = christian_relics_2a
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = christian_relics_2b

			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.301.capital

			limit = { FROM = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 5 } } }

				FROM = { change_variable = { which = christian_relics value = -5 } }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 4 } } }
			dg_add_prestige = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				capital_scope = { change_variable = { which = christian_relics value = 4 } }
				FROM = { change_variable = { which = christian_relics value = -4 } }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 3 } } }
			dg_add_prestige_small = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				capital_scope = { change_variable = { which = christian_relics value = 3 } }
				FROM = { change_variable = { which = christian_relics value = -3 } }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 2 } } }
			dg_add_prestige_small = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				capital_scope = { change_variable = { which = christian_relics value = 2 } }
				FROM = { change_variable = { which = christian_relics value = -2 } }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 1 } } }
			dg_add_prestige_small = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				capital_scope = { change_variable = { which = christian_relics value = 1 } }
				FROM = { change_variable = { which = christian_relics value = -1 } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.301.elsewhere
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				is_capital = no
				is_in_capital_area = yes
				OR = {
					has_owner_religion = yes
					temple_trigger = yes
				}
				controlled_by = owner
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = pilgrimage_route }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40

					}

			}
		}
		else_if = {

			dg_add_prestige_small = yes
			add_treasury = -15
			random_owned_province = {

				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_variable_equal = { which = christian_relics value = 2 } } }
			dg_add_prestige_small = yes

			random_owned_province = {

			dg_add_prestige_small = yes
			add_treasury = -5
			random_owned_province = {

country_event = { #303 - Papal Tribute
	
	id = dg_catholic.303
	title = dg_catholic.303.t
	desc = dg_catholic.303.d
	picture = catholic_reliquary_saffron # pending a better choice of picture by David
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #By dg_conversion.001 for ENG only in early starts
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = papal_fiefdom_ENG
		OR = {
			tag = ENG
			tag = GBR
		}
		religion = catholic
		is_papal_controller = no
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.303.never #1365
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				NOT = { papal_influence = 1 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { prestige = 0 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				any_rival_country = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		add_papal_influence = -10
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = disobeyed_religious_leader }
		add_prestige = 10
		clr_country_flag = papal_fiefdom_ENG
		set_country_flag = papal_interference
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.303.no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				NOT = { papal_influence = 1 }
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		add_papal_influence = -5
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.303.pay #Last paid in 1333
		trigger = { treasury = 5 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				num_of_loans = 1
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_loans = 2
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_loans = 3
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { treasury = 25 }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { treasury = 50 }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				papal_influence = 200
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_papal_influence = 5
		add_prestige = -5
		add_treasury = -5
		PAP = { add_treasury = 5 }
	}
}

		NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }

			}
		}

			factor = 1.4
		}

			has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
			factor = 0.5
		}

			has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			is_papal_controller = yes
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.031.a #Pay the tithe
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				years_of_income = 0.5
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				years_of_income = 1
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				years_of_income = 2
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { years_of_income = 0.10 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { years_of_income = 0.25 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_loans = 1
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_loans = 2
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				is_bankrupt = yes
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }
		if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 500 }
			add_treasury = -500

			limit = { monthly_income = 5 }
			add_years_of_income = -0.08
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = -5
		}
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = 2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = 1.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = 1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = 0.5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.031.b #Make the peasants pay
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }

	option = {

			modifier = {

			}

				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = disobeyed_religious_leader }

		}
		else_if = {

province_event = { #Jesuit Missionaries
	
	id = dg_catholic.034
	title = dg_catholic.034.t
	desc = dg_catholic.034.d
	picture = catholic_monks_preaching
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 } }
		NOT = { religion_years = { protestant = 80 } }
		owner = { religion = catholic }
		PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 200 } }
		owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = jesuits_suppressed } }
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = jesuit_activity }
		religion_group = christian
		owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated } }
		OR = {
			is_in_capital_area = yes
			culture_group = owner
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_missionaries value = 1 } }
				owner = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 } }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = protestant value = 12 }
					check_variable = { which = reformed value = 12 }
					check_variable = { which = hussite value = 20 }
					check_variable = { which = gnostic value = 20 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_missionaries value = 1 } }
				owner = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 2 } }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = protestant value = 8 }
					check_variable = { which = reformed value = 8 }
					check_variable = { which = hussite value = 16 }
					check_variable = { which = gnostic value = 16 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_missionaries value = 2 } }
				owner = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 3 } }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = protestant value = 4 }
					check_variable = { which = reformed value = 4 }
					check_variable = { which = hussite value = 12 }
					check_variable = { which = gnostic value = 12 }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_missionaries value = 2 } }
				owner = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 4 } }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = protestant value = 4 }
					check_variable = { which = reformed value = 4 }
					check_variable = { which = hussite value = 8 }
					check_variable = { which = gnostic value = 8 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 20
		
		modifier = {
			PAP = { has_country_flag = jesuits_limited }
			owner = { has_country_flag = ally_of_pope }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			PAP = { has_country_flag = jesuits_limited }
			owner = { has_country_flag = friend_of_pope }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			PAP = { has_country_flag = jesuits_limited }
			owner = { has_country_flag = rival_of_pope }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			PAP = { has_country_flag = jesuits_limited }
			owner = { has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 2 } }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 3 } }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 4 } }
			factor = 0.7

		modifier = {

			factor = 0.7
		}

			factor = 2

			factor = 0.7
		}
	}
	
	option = {

country_event = { #Jesuit Education
	
	id = dg_catholic.035
	title = dg_catholic.035.t
	desc = dg_catholic.035.d
	picture = catholic_monks
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
		is_at_war = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = dg_jesuit_education }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = jesuits_suppressed }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 20
		
		modifier = {
			PAP = { has_country_flag = jesuits_limited }
			has_country_flag = ally_of_pope
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			PAP = { has_country_flag = jesuits_limited }
			has_country_flag = friend_of_pope
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			PAP = { has_country_flag = jesuits_limited }
			has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			PAP = { has_country_flag = jesuits_limited }
			has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 2 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_country_flag = dg_jesuit_education }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.035.a #Establish a Jesuit college
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 } }
		add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
		add_piety = 0.05
		add_adm_power = 25
		set_country_flag = jesuit_colleges
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.035.b #Let them run our entire school system
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = public_religious_schools } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = preparatory_schools
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_modifier = dg_public_schools
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 } }
		add_piety = 0.10
		add_adm_power = 50
		set_country_flag = jesuit_colleges
		add_country_modifier = { name = jesuit_schools duration = -1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = monastic_schools }
			remove_country_modifier = monastic_schools
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = charity_schools }
			remove_country_modifier = charity_schools
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = dg_public_schools }
			remove_country_modifier = dg_public_schools
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = preparatory_schools }
			remove_country_modifier = preparatory_schools
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.10
		}
		else = {
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.035.c #We have no interest in this arrangement
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Papal Legate arrives in $CAPITAL$
	
	id = dg_catholic.036
	title = dg_catholic.036.t
	desc = dg_catholic.036.d
	picture = catholic_papal_legate
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction
			has_country_flag = national_church
		}
		religion = catholic
		OR = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.60
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = concordat_of_bologna }
		is_papal_controller = no
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { years = 41 }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.036.a #We will not change our minds
		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -1
		}
		add_papal_influence = -5
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = disobeyed_religious_leader }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.036.b #Restore papal sovereignty over $COUNTRY$
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = 0.20 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = excommunicated
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = dispensation_denied
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = church_autonomy_revoked
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction
			clr_country_flag = national_church
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_denied #Gives a second chance to clear your name now
			set_country_flag = dispensation_granted #Gives a massive bonus to your chance of success next time you need dispensation
		}
		add_papal_influence = 25
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }
	}
}

country_event = { #37 - The Roman Inquisition
	
	id = dg_catholic.037
	title = dg_catholic.037.t
	desc = dg_catholic.037.d
	picture = catholic_heretic_scientist
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		NOT = { has_country_flag = roman_inquisition }
		any_neighbor_country = {
			religion = catholic
			has_country_flag = roman_inquisition
			check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 2 }
		}
		piety = -0.60
		OR = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.60
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 8
		
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.037.a #We welcome this news
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 2 } }
		set_country_flag = roman_inquisition
		add_papal_influence = 25
		add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.037.b #We shall redouble our efforts
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 1 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 2 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = roman_inquisition
			change_variable = { which = inquisition value = 1 }
		}
		add_papal_influence = 10
		add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.037.c #Introduce an inquisition to $COUNTRY$
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 1 } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = roman_inquisition
			change_variable = { which = inquisition value = 2 }
		}
		add_papal_influence = 10
		add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = obeyed_religious_leader }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.037.e #Reject the idea
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				NOT = { PAP = { culture_group = ROOT } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				government = theocracy
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 1 } } }
		set_country_flag = roman_inquisition
		add_papal_influence = -10
		add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = disobeyed_religious_leader }
	}
}

country_event = { #38 - Forbidden Books
	
	id = dg_catholic.038
	title = dg_catholic.038.t
	desc = dg_catholic.038.d
	picture = all_publishing
	
	trigger = {
		any_neighbor_country = { has_country_flag = forbidden_index }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = forbidden_index }
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			AND = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					primary_culture = ROOT
					religion = catholic
					has_country_flag = forbidden_index_banned
				}
				OR = {
					religion = protestant
					religion = reformed
					religion = hussite
					religion = gnostic
				}
			}
		}
		PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } }
		piety = -0.60
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 25
		
		modifier = {
			any_neighbor_country = { has_country_flag = forbidden_index_banned }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { religion = catholic }
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = forbidden_index } }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.038.a #Enforce the ban by law
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = introduce_reformation
					has_country_flag = spread_reformation
					has_country_flag = reformation_maybe
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 1 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 2 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				overlord = { has_country_flag = forbidden_index_banned }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		trigger = { religion = catholic }
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = forbidden_index_banned }
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_stability_1 = yes
		}
		else = {
			subtract_stability_1 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 2 } } }
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
		}
		add_adm_power = -10
		add_papal_influence = 10
		if = {
			limit = { advisor = philosopher }
			remove_advisor = philosopher
			define_advisor = { religion = catholic type = inquisitor discount = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.038.b #Make a show of burning a few books
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		trigger = { religion = catholic }
		add_treasury = -5
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.038.c #Reject the authority of the pope
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				religion = catholic
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				religion = catholic
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				religion = catholic
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = introduce_reformation
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = spread_reformation
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { religion = catholic government = theocracy }
			NOT = { religion = catholic check_variable = { which = inquisition value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { religion = catholic }
			add_papal_influence = -10
			if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 500 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 500 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 500 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.038.e #Print the books for foreign consumption
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				religion = reformed
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { religion = catholic }
			any_neighbor_country = {
				primary_culture = ROOT
				religion = catholic
				has_country_flag = forbidden_index_banned
			}
		}
		random_neighbor_country = {
			limit = { primary_culture = ROOT religion = catholic has_country_flag = forbidden_index_banned }
			add_casus_belli = { target = ROOT type = cb_insult months = 60 }
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				culture_group = owner
				any_neighbor_province = { culture = ROOT NOT = { owned_by = ROOT } }
				num_free_building_slots = 1
				NOT = { has_building = workshop }
			}
			add_building = workshop
			owner = { add_treasury = -10 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #A Cry For Help
	
	id = dg_catholic.041

		NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = crusade_demand } } #Only one crusade at a time

				}

			religion = catholic
			factor = 0.7

		modifier = {

			religion = catholic
			factor = 0.7

			has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { religion = catholic }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			government = theocracy
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } } }
			factor = 1.4

			PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = crusade_denied
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { PAP = { set_country_flag = crusade_demand } }
	}
	
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			#Likely to lose the war

				NOT = { num_of_cities = 3 }
				any_known_country = {
					war_with = ROOT
					NOT = { religion_group = christian }
					is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
					num_of_cities = 5
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { num_of_cities = 5 }
				any_known_country = {
					war_with = ROOT
					NOT = { religion_group = christian }
					is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
					num_of_cities = 10
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}

				NOT = { num_of_cities = 10 }
				any_known_country = {
					war_with = ROOT
					NOT = { religion_group = christian }

				NOT = { num_of_cities = 20 }

					war_with = ROOT
					NOT = { religion_group = christian }
					is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
					num_of_cities = 40
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { num_of_cities = 40 }
				any_known_country = {
					war_with = ROOT
					NOT = { religion_group = christian }
					is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
					num_of_cities = 80
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.50 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.25 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.10 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			#Likely to win the war
			modifier = {
				manpower_percentage = 0.75
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				manpower_percentage = 0.90
				factor = 0.7
			}
			#Losing the war
			modifier = {
				any_owned_province = { NOT = { controlled_by = owner } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { war_score = -25 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { war_score = -50 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			#Likely to get a crusade or humble
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = crusade_promised
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { prestige = 0 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { prestige = -50 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = friend_of_pope
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = ally_of_pope
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				is_papal_controller = yes
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				papal_trigger = yes
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			#Not likely to get a crusade or too proud
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = crusade_denied
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				prestige = 50
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				prestige = 25
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { religion = catholic }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = { #Winning the war
				war_score = 1
				factor = 0.7
			}
			#Wants a crusade
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { religion = catholic }
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			#Doesn't want a crusade
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { religion = catholic }
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { religion = catholic }
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_known_country = {
				limit = {
					war_with = ROOT
					NOT = { religion_group = christian }
					is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
					#Because the game is sometimes stupid:
					#num_of_cities = 1
					NOT = { tag = REB }
				}
				set_country_flag = crusade_target
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { religion_group = christian }
				set_variable = { which = crusade_goal value = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_owner_culture = yes }
					change_variable = { which = crusade_goal value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_in_capital_area = yes }
					change_variable = { which = crusade_goal value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_capital = yes }
					change_variable = { which = crusade_goal value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { controller = { NOT = { religion_group = ROOT } } }
					change_variable = { which = crusade_goal value = 2 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { any_neighbor_province = { owner = { war_with = ROOT NOT = { religion_group = ROOT } } } }
					change_variable = { which = crusade_goal value = 2 }
				}
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					all_owned_province = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = crusade_goal which = PREV } }
							is_variable_equal = { which = crusade_goal which = PREV }
						}
					}
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = catholic_crusade_goal
			}
			every_owned_province = { set_variable = { which = crusade_goal value = 0 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -8
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = crusade_sponsor }
		if = { #Skips the normal process
			limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
			add_manpower = 1
			add_country_modifier = { name = morale_boost duration = 100 }
			hidden_effect = {
				PAP = {
					clr_country_flag = crusade_demand
					set_country_flag = crusade_called
					set_country_flag = crusader
				}
				set_country_flag = crusader
			}
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_target }
			country_event = { id = dg_catholic.042 days = 90 }
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
			country_event = { id = dg_pope.013 days = 30 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { religion = catholic }
				set_country_flag = renaissance
				#if = {
				#	limit = { has_country_flag = humanism }
					clr_country_flag = humanism
				#}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_owner_culture = yes
						is_core = owner
						has_province_flag = humanism
					}
					clr_province_flag = humanism
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.041.b #We can fight them ourselves
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = { clr_country_flag = crusade_demand }
			set_country_flag = crusade_rejected
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Christian crusade against $COUNTRY$
	
	id = dg_catholic.042
	title = dg_catholic.042.t
	desc = dg_catholic.042.d
	picture = catholic_crusade
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.042.a #Let them come!
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = morale_boost duration = 200 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = morale_boost duration = 100 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = morale_boost duration = 50 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = morale_boost duration = 25 }
		}
	}
}

				random_known_country = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor }
					reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = crusade_supported }
					hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 2 } } }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = -1
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor }
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = crusade_supported }
				hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 1 } } }
			}
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = crusade_target
				#num_of_cities = 1
				NOT = { tag = REB }
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = crusade_target }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.043.c #Let them fend for themselves
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_known_country = { has_country_flag = crusade_target religion = hussite }
					any_known_country = { has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor has_country_flag = internal_crusade }
				}
				has_country_flag = hussite_persecution
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_known_country = { has_country_flag = crusade_target religion = hussite }
					any_known_country = { has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor has_country_flag = internal_crusade }
				}
				has_country_flag = hussite_confederation
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = -1
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = crusade_refused }
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor }
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = crusade_rejected }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.043.e #Tell the pope the age of crusades is over
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = PAP }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				any_neighbor_country = { has_country_flag = crusade_target }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -12
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -9
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = -6
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = crusades_over }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor
					papal_trigger = yes
					is_papal_controller = yes
				}
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = crusade_rejected }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.043.f #The age of crusades is over (Papacy)
		trigger = {
			tag = PAP
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -30
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -24
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -18
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = -12
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = crusades_over }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor
					papal_trigger = yes
					is_papal_controller = yes
				}
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = crusade_rejected }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Crusade called (notifier)
	
	id = dg_catholic.044
	title = dg_catholic.044.t
	desc = dg_catholic.044.d
	picture = catholic_crusade
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #By dg_pope.013
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.044.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_papal_controller = yes
					tag = PAP
				}
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = papacy_great }
		}
		add_yearly_manpower = 1
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_war_exhaustion = -4
				add_country_modifier = { name = morale_boost duration = 800 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_war_exhaustion = -3
				add_country_modifier = { name = morale_boost duration = 600 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_war_exhaustion = -2
				add_country_modifier = { name = morale_boost duration = 400 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_war_exhaustion = -1
				add_country_modifier = { name = morale_boost duration = 200 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_war_exhaustion = -1
			add_country_modifier = { name = morale_boost duration = 200 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Crusade denied (notifier)
	
	id = dg_catholic.045
	title = dg_catholic.045.t
	desc = dg_catholic.045.d
	picture = catholic_papal_legate
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #By dg_pope.013
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.045.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				piety = 0.60
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_morale duration = 400 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_morale duration = 300 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_morale duration = 200 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_morale duration = 100 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_morale duration = 100 }
		}
	}
}

			}
