			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -1 } } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.046.c #Accept their generous donations
		trigger = { PAP = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = crusade_manpower value = 1 } } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = crusader }
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = crusade_supported }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 512 } } }
			add_treasury = 512
			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -512 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 256 } }
			}
			add_treasury = 256
			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -256 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 128 } }
			}
			add_treasury = 128
			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -128 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 64 } }
			}
			add_treasury = 64
			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -64 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 32 } }
			}
			add_treasury = 32
			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -32 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 16 } }
			}
			add_treasury = 16
			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -16 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 8 } }
			}
			add_treasury = 8
			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -8 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 4 } }
			}
			add_treasury = 4
			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -4 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 2 } }
			}
			add_treasury = 2
			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -2 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = 1 } }
			}
			add_treasury = 1
			hidden_effect = { PAP = { change_variable = { which = crusade_funding value = -1 } } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Crusade ends prematurely
	
	id = dg_catholic.047
	title = dg_catholic.047.t
	desc = dg_catholic.047.d
	picture = catholic_papal_legate
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #By dg_pope.001
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.047.a
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = crusade_sponsor }
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_morale duration = 800 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_morale duration = 600 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_morale duration = 400 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_morale duration = 200 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = decreased_morale duration = 200 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				#limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_refused }
				clr_country_flag = crusade_refused
				clr_country_flag = crusade_supporter
				clr_country_flag = crusade_target
				clr_country_flag = crusade_sponsor
				clr_country_flag = crusader
			}
			#every_country = {
			#	limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_supporter }
			#	clr_country_flag = crusade_supporter
			#}
			#every_country = {
			#	limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_target }
			#	clr_country_flag = crusade_target
			#}
			#every_country = {
			#	limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor }
			#	clr_country_flag = crusade_sponsor
			#}
			#every_country = {
			#	limit = { has_country_flag = crusader }
			#	clr_country_flag = crusader
			#}
			PAP = { clr_country_flag = crusade_called }
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Crusade of $PROVINCENAME$ ends
	
	id = dg_catholic.048
	title = dg_catholic.048.t
	desc = dg_catholic.048.d
	picture = catholic_crusade_successful
	
	trigger = {
		has_saved_event_target = catholic_crusade_goal
		event_target:catholic_crusade_goal = { province_id = ROOT }
		PAP = { has_country_flag = crusade_called }
		owner = {
			religion_group = christian
			NOT = { has_country_flag = was_catholic }
			is_force_converted = no
			at_war_with_religious_enemy = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = internal_crusade }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.048.a
		owner = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = crusade_supporter
						has_country_flag = crusader
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = crusade_supporter
				clr_country_flag = crusader
				hidden_effect = {
					reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = crusade_supported }
					add_prestige = 1
					change_variable = { which = crusades_fought value = -0.5 }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = crusades_fought value = -1 }
				regiongroup = {
					region = {
						limit = { has_province_flag = crusade_goal }
						clr_province_flag = crusade_goal
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					#limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_refused }
					clr_country_flag = crusade_refused
					clr_country_flag = crusade_target
					clr_country_flag = crusade_sponsor
				}
				#every_country = {
				#	limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_target }
				#	clr_country_flag = crusade_target
				#}
				#every_country = {
				#	limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor }
				#	clr_country_flag = crusade_sponsor
				#}
				PAP = { clr_country_flag = crusade_called }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Crusade ends in defeat
	
	id = dg_catholic.049
	title = dg_catholic.049.t
	desc = dg_catholic.049.d
	picture = catholic_burning_church
	
	trigger = {
		has_saved_event_target = catholic_crusade_goal
		PAP = { has_country_flag = crusade_called }
		OR = {
			NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = crusade_leader_sought } }
			PAP = { had_country_flag = { flag = crusade_leader_sought days = 1000 } }
		}
		NOT = { event_target:catholic_crusade_goal = { owner = { religion = catholic is_excommunicated = no } } }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor
				NOT = { has_country_flag = internal_crusade }
				NOT = { any_known_country = { has_country_flag = crusade_target war_with = ROOT } }
			}
			AND = {
				is_papal_controller = yes
				NOT = { any_known_country = { has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor } }
				OR = {
					NOT = { any_known_country = { has_country_flag = internal_crusade } }
					any_known_country = { had_country_flag = { flag = internal_crusade days = 1000 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.049.a
		add_prestige = -5
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = internal_crusade
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = crusades_fought value = 3 } }
				}
				clr_country_flag = internal_crusade
				set_country_flag = internal_crusade
			}
			regiongroup = {
				region = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = crusade_goal }
					clr_province_flag = crusade_goal
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				#limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_refused }
				clr_country_flag = crusade_refused
				clr_country_flag = crusade_supporter
				clr_country_flag = crusade_target
				clr_country_flag = crusade_sponsor
				clr_country_flag = crusader
			}
			#every_country = {
			#	limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_supporter }
			#	clr_country_flag = crusade_supporter
			#}
			#every_country = {
			#	limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_target }
			#	clr_country_flag = crusade_target
			#}
			#every_country = {
			#	limit = { has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor }
			#	clr_country_flag = crusade_sponsor
			#}
			#every_country = {
			#	limit = { has_country_flag = crusader }
			#	clr_country_flag = crusader
			#}
			PAP = { clr_country_flag = crusade_called }
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Church council called
	
	id = dg_catholic.052
	title = dg_catholic.052.t
	desc = dg_catholic.052.d
	picture = catholic_church_council
	
	trigger = {
		PAP = { has_country_flag = church_council_called }
		NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = council_site_chosen } }
		religion = catholic
		continent = europe
		owner = { religion = catholic }
		owner = { piety = -0.20 }
		owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated } }
		owner = { is_at_war = no }
		has_siege = no
		controlled_by = owner
		is_city = yes
		has_owner_culture = yes
		NOT = { unrest = 5 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 83
		
		#A neutral site is preferred (not a great power or the pope)
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 40 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 20 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 10 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { num_of_cities = 5 }
			factor = 1.6
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { NOT = { num_of_cities = 3 } }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = ally_of_pope }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = friend_of_pope }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = rival_of_pope }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { tag = PAP }
			factor = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { tag = PAP }
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 1 } }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { tag = PAP }
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 2 } }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { tag = PAP }
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 3 } }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { tag = PAP }
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 4 } }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { tag = PAP }
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 5 } }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { tag = PAP }
			PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 6 } }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { is_papal_controller = yes }
			factor = 3
		}
		#A safe site is preferred
		modifier = {
			unrest = 1
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			unrest = 3
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			any_neighbor_province = { has_siege = yes }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			any_neighbor_province = { NOT = { controlled_by = owner } }
			factor = 2
		}
		#Other factors
		modifier = {
			NOT = { owner = { capital_distance = { who = PAP distance = 130 } } }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { capital_distance = { who = PAP distance = 260 } }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { capital_distance = { who = PAP distance = 390 } }
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			PAP = { has_country_flag = church_council_delays }
			factor = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			exists = AVI
			AVI = { papal_trigger = yes }
			factor = 0.25
		}
		modifier = {
			is_religion_enabled = protestant
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			is_religion_enabled = reformed
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = renaissance }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_flag = renaissance_ideas
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = humanism }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_flag = humanist_ideas
			factor = 1.4
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.052.a #Host the council in $PROVINCENAME$
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = humanism }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_province_flag = humanist_ideas
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = renaissance }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_province_flag = renaissance_ideas
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_owner_culture = yes
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		set_province_flag = church_council_site
		add_province_modifier = { name = church_council_preparations duration = 100 }
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = { set_country_flag = council_site_chosen }
			save_global_event_target_as = council_site
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = catholic
					OR = {
						num_of_cities = 10
						is_papal_controller = yes
						papal_trigger = yes
					}
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				country_event = { id = dg_catholic.053 days = 30 } #Council site proposed
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.052.b #Suggest an alternative
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Council site proposed
	
	id = dg_catholic.053
	title = dg_catholic.053.t
	desc = dg_catholic.052.d
	picture = catholic_building_project
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		custom_tooltip = dg_catholic.052.d2
		hidden_effect = {
			#So options show up in event
			if = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				FROM = { owner = { change_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 1 } } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { papal_trigger = yes }
				FROM = { owner = { change_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 1 } } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { num_of_cities = 10 }
				FROM = { owner = { change_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 1 } } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { num_of_cities = 25 }
				FROM = { owner = { change_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 1 } } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { num_of_cities = 50 }
				FROM = { owner = { change_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 1 } } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.053.a #It is acceptable to us
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		FROM = { owner = { add_prestige = 1 } }
		#Correction
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				FROM = { owner = { change_variable = { which = council_boycott value = -1 } } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { papal_trigger = yes }
				FROM = { owner = { change_variable = { which = council_boycott value = -1 } } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { num_of_cities = 50 }
				FROM = { owner = { change_variable = { which = council_boycott value = -3 } } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { num_of_cities = 25 }
				FROM = { owner = { change_variable = { which = council_boycott value = -2 } } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { num_of_cities = 10 }
				FROM = { owner = { change_variable = { which = council_boycott value = -1 } } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.053.b #Refuse to attend this council
		trigger = {
			NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 5 } } }
			OR = {
				FROM = { owner = { is_rival = ROOT } }
				FROM = { owner = { is_enemy = ROOT } }
				FROM = { owner = { war_with = ROOT } }
				FROM = { owner = { truce_with = ROOT } }
				ai = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 1 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 2 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 3 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 4 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 5 } }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT } }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { culture_group = ROOT } }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { alliance_with = ROOT } }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { marriage_with = ROOT } }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { is_enemy = ROOT } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { owner = { war_with = ROOT } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = council_boycott_explained
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = council_boycott }
		FROM = {
			owner = {
				add_prestige = -1
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = religious_scandal_pious }
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #Unsuitable council site
	
	id = dg_catholic.054
	title = dg_catholic.054.t
	desc = dg_catholic.054.d
	picture = catholic_church_trial
	
	trigger = {
		had_province_flag = { flag = church_council_site days = 50 }
		owner = { check_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 4 } }
		OR = {
			NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } } }
			AND = {
				NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } } }
				owner = { check_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 6 } }
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } } }
				owner = { check_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 8 } }
			}
			AND = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } }
				owner = { check_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 10 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.054.a #Too bad!
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = { change_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 1 } }
			regiongroup = {
				region = {
					clr_province_flag = church_council_site
				}
			} #Just in case
			PAP = { clr_country_flag = council_site_chosen }
			owner = { set_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 0 } }
			PAP = { set_variable = { which = council_boycott value = 0 } }
		}
		remove_province_modifier = church_council_preparations
		#	FROM = { add_papal_influence = -1 }
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				#limit = { has_country_flag = council_boycott }
				clr_country_flag = council_boycott
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #The council of $PROVINCECAPITAL$ begins
	
	id = dg_catholic.055
	title = dg_catholic.055.t
	desc = dg_catholic.055.d
	picture = catholic_church_council
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = church_council_site
		PAP = { has_country_flag = council_site_chosen }
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = church_council_preparations }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			regiongroup = {
				region = {
					clr_province_flag = church_council_site
				}
			} #Just in case
			set_province_flag = church_council
			PAP = {
				set_country_flag = church_council
				clr_country_flag = church_council_delays
				clr_country_flag = reformation_council_called
				clr_country_flag = church_council_called
				clr_country_flag = reformation_council_demands
				clr_country_flag = reformation_council_begging
				set_variable = { which = church_council_frustration value = 0 }
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = church_council duration = 1000 }
		add_province_modifier = { name = church_council_opening_session duration = 100 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.055.a
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				clr_country_flag = council_host_country
				clr_country_flag = council_site_approved
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { has_country_flag = council_boycott }
				is_papal_controller = no
				OR = {
					is_at_war = no
					government = theocracy
					has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = dg_catholic.056 days = 30 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				#limit = { has_country_flag = council_boycott }
				clr_country_flag = council_boycott
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Church council begins
	
	id = dg_catholic.056
	title = dg_catholic.056.t
	desc = dg_catholic.056.d
	picture = catholic_church_council
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #By dg_catholic.055
	
	immediate = {
		custom_tooltip = dg_reform_desire_explained
		if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = reform_desire_indulgences value = 1 } }
				NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = indulgences_banned } }
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_reform_desire_indulgences
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = reform_desire_simony value = 1 } }
				OR = {
					NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = simony_abolished } }
					NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = annate_abolished } }
				}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {

					NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = clerical_residence } }
					NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = seminaries } }
				}

		}

			limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = reform_desire_conciliarism value = 1 } } }
			custom_tooltip = dg_reform_desire_conciliarism
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.056.a #Send them without instructions
		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.056.b #Try to mend the schism
		trigger = {
			exists = AVI
			AVI = { papal_trigger = yes religion = catholic }
			exists = PAP

		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {

				}

					limit = {
						num_of_cities = 32
					}
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = council_schism value = 7 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						num_of_cities = 22
					}
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = council_schism value = 6 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						num_of_cities = 14
					}
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = council_schism value = 5 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						num_of_cities = 8
					}
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = council_schism value = 4 } }
				}

					limit = {
						num_of_cities = 4

province_event = { #The council of $PROVINCENAME$ ends (deadlock)
	
	id = dg_catholic.057
	title = dg_catholic.057.t
	desc = dg_catholic.057.d
	picture = catholic_church_trial
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = church_council
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = church_council }
		NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = council_accomplishments } }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = {
				clr_country_flag = church_council_topics_chosen
				clr_country_flag = council_site_chosen
				clr_country_flag = church_council
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.057.a
		hidden_effect = { clr_province_flag = church_council }
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = attend_council
				}
				if = {
					limit = { piety = 0.60 }
					add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = council_failed_fanatical }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { piety = 0.20 }
					add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = council_failed_pious }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { piety = -0.20 }
					add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = council_failed_observant }
				}
				clr_country_flag = attend_council
			}
			PAP = { clr_country_flag = council_accomplishments }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_papal_controller = yes
						tag = PAP
						AND = {
							religion = catholic
							has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
						}
					}
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				country_event = { id = dg_catholic.111 }
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #The council of $PROVINCENAME$ ends (success)
	
	id = dg_catholic.058
	title = dg_catholic.058.t
	desc = dg_catholic.058.d
	picture = catholic_church_council
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = church_council
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = church_council }
		PAP = { has_country_flag = council_accomplishments }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = {
				clr_country_flag = church_council_topics_chosen
				clr_country_flag = council_site_chosen
				clr_country_flag = church_council
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.058.a
		hidden_effect = { clr_province_flag = church_council }
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = 3
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = 2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = attend_council }
				if = {
					limit = { piety = 0.60 }
					add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = council_succeeded_fanatical }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { piety = 0.20 }
					add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = council_succeeded_pious }
				}
				clr_country_flag = attend_council
			}
			PAP = { clr_country_flag = council_accomplishments }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_papal_controller = yes
						tag = PAP
						AND = {
							religion = catholic
							has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
						}
					}
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				country_event = { id = dg_catholic.112 }
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #The council of $PROVINCENAME$ ends (threat of war)
	
	id = dg_catholic.059
	title = dg_catholic.059.t
	desc = dg_catholic.059.d
	picture = catholic_church_council
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = church_council
		has_province_modifier = church_council
		OR = {
			has_siege = yes
			NOT = { controlled_by = owner }
			any_neighbor_province = { has_siege = yes }
			any_neighbor_province = { controlled_by = REB }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 12
		
		modifier = {
			has_siege = yes
			factor = 0.2
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { controlled_by = owner }
			factor = 0.1
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = {
				clr_country_flag = church_council_topics_chosen
				clr_country_flag = council_site_chosen
				clr_country_flag = church_council
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.059.a
		remove_province_modifier = church_council
		hidden_effect = { clr_province_flag = church_council }
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -3
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = attend_council }
				if = {
					limit = { piety = 0.60 }
					add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = council_failed_fanatical }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { piety = 0.20 }
					add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = council_failed_pious }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { piety = -0.20 }
					add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = council_failed_observant }
				}
				clr_country_flag = attend_council
			}
			PAP = {
				clr_country_flag = council_accomplishments
				clr_country_flag = church_council
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_papal_controller = yes
						tag = PAP
						AND = {
							religion = catholic
							has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
						}
					}
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				country_event = { id = dg_catholic.113 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #$MONARCH$'s shame
	
	id = dg_catholic.061
	title = dg_catholic.061.t
	desc = dg_catholic.061.d
	picture = catholic_trial
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation }
				}
				change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 4 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = great_matter
			set_country_flag = royal_scandal
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_religion_enabled = protestant
					NOT = { has_country_flag = protestant_reaction }
					has_country_flag = renaissance
				}
				clr_country_flag = renaissance
				capital_scope = { clr_province_flag = renaissance_ideas }
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.061.a #Wait for the scandal to die down
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 800 }
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 1600 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 400 }
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 800 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 200 }
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 400 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 100 }
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_province duration = 200 }
			}
		}
		dg_reduce_legitimacy_large = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Scandal abates
	
	id = dg_catholic.062
	title = dg_catholic.062.t
	desc = dg_catholic.062.d
	picture = catholic_scandal
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = royal_scandal
		NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 10
		
		modifier = {
			NOT = { religion = catholic }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = dispensation_denied
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { legitimacy = 80 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { legitimacy = 60 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { legitimacy = 40 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { legitimacy = 20 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			stability = 1
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			stability = 3
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { stability = 0 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { stability = -2 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.062.a #Finally!
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_denied
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_process
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_consideration
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_granted
			clr_country_flag = excommunicated
			clr_country_flag = royal_scandal
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_bribe
			clr_country_flag = unfair_excommunication
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_sponsoring_schism
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_secular_Rome
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_rome
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_reformation
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_usurp_church
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Dispensation Granted
	
	id = dg_catholic.063
	title = dg_catholic.063.t
	desc = dg_catholic.063.d
	picture = catholic_papal_envoy
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = excommunicated
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = diplomatic_excommunication
			is_papal_controller = yes
		}
		religion = catholic
		is_excommunicated = no
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	#is_triggered_only = yes #By dg_pope.011
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.063.a #Our good name is restored
		add_opinion = { who = PAP modifier = papacy_good }
		dg_add_legitimacy_large = yes
		dg_add_prestige_small = yes
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_modifier
			religious_scandal_country_strong = {
				remove_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
			}
			religious_scandal_country = {
				remove_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
			}
			religious_scandal_country_weak = {
				remove_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = dispensation_consideration value = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_denied
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_process
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_consideration
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_granted
			clr_country_flag = begged_for_dispensation
			clr_country_flag = excommunicated
			clr_country_flag = royal_scandal
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_bribe
			clr_country_flag = unfair_excommunication
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_sponsoring_schism
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_secular_Rome
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_rome
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_reformation
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_usurp_church
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Dispensation denied
	
	id = dg_catholic.065
	title = dg_catholic.065.t
	desc = dg_catholic.065.d
	picture = catholic_excommunication
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #By dg_pope.011
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_eccleistical_courts value = 0.1 } }
				}
			}
			add_reform_desire = 0.001
		}
		else = { #Invention of the printing press in 1450 allows for much faster and cheaper communication of problems
			random = {
				chance = 25
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_simony value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
				add_reform_desire = 0.001
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation }
				}
				change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					war_with = PAP
					truce_with = PAP
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = denied_PAP_war
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_owned_province = { is_core = PAP } NOT = { tag = PAP }
					owns_rome_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = denied_occupying_PAP
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope }
			custom_tooltip = denied_enemy_of_pope
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_ally = { NOT = { religion = catholic } } }
			custom_tooltip = denied_heretic_alliance
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
					religion = catholic
					NOT = { is_core = owner }
					value = 3
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = denied_conquests
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { piety = -0.20 } }
			custom_tooltip = denied_lack_of_piety
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 } }
			custom_tooltip = denied_lack_of_church_influence
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { DIP = 2 } }
			custom_tooltip = denied_monarch_DIP
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.065.a #Damnation!
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_process
			clr_country_flag = dispensation_consideration
			set_country_flag = dispensation_denied
		}
		dg_reduce_legitimacy = yes
		dg_reduce_prestige_small = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Excommunication
	
	id = dg_catholic.066
	title = dg_catholic.066.t
	desc = dg_catholic.066.d
	picture = catholic_excommunication
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #By dg_pope.027
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = tolerant_hre }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_conversion
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = sheltered_luther }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_conversion
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { religion = catholic } has_country_flag = was_catholic }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_conversion
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_rome }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_rome
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_church }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_church
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_heathen_ally
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_blasphemy
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_papal_states
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_unjust_war
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.066.b #Give back Rome
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		trigger = { has_country_flag = excommunication_rome }
		2530 = { cede_province = PAP }
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_rome
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_church
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 0 }
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				set_country_flag = excommunication_repented
				country_event = { id = dg_pope.028 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.066.c #End our alliance
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		trigger = { has_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally }
		random_ally = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
				is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
				any_known_country = { war_with = PREV religion = catholic }
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = heathen_friendship_broken }
		}
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_rome
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_church
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 0 }
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				set_country_flag = excommunication_repented
				country_event = { id = dg_pope.028 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.066.e #Leave the Papal States
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		trigger = { has_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { is_core = PAP NOT = { is_core = owner } }
			cede_province = PAP
		}
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_rome
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_church
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 0 }
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				set_country_flag = excommunication_repented
				country_event = { id = dg_pope.028 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.066.f #Have our cardinals argue our case
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			num_of_cardinals = 1
			papal_influence = 20
			OR = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 2 } }
				AND = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 3 } }
					num_of_cardinals = 3
					papal_influence = 20
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 2 } }
			add_papal_influence = -40
			add_country_modifier = { name = excommunication_reprieve duration = 2000 }
		}
		else = {
			add_papal_influence = -20
			add_country_modifier = { name = excommunication_reprieve duration = 2000 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 0 }
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				set_country_flag = excommunication_argued
				country_event = { id = dg_pope.028 days = 30 }
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_rome
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_church
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.066.g #Switch allegiance to the Anti-Pope
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		trigger = {
			AVI = {
				num_of_cities = 1
				papal_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = support_antipope
		clr_country_flag = support_roman_pope
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 0 } }
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_rome
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_church
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.066.a #Suffer this indignity
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy }
			set_country_flag = catholic_blasphemy #This can never happen again to the same country
		}
		set_country_flag = excommunicated
		clr_country_flag = repress_protestants_abroad
		clr_country_flag = counter_reformation
		clr_country_flag = catholic_reformation
		clr_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation
		clr_country_flag = reformation_maybe
		clr_country_flag = introduce_reformation
		clr_country_flag = spread_reformation
		clr_country_flag = refused_reformation
		clr_country_flag = renaissance
		set_country_flag = former_excommunication_target
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				OR = {
					war_with = ROOT
					alliance_with = ROOT
					junior_union_with = ROOT
					senior_union_with = ROOT
					vassal_of = ROOT
					overlord_of = ROOT
					has_country_flag = religious_news_all
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							marriage_with = ROOT
							truce_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					AND = {
						religion = catholic
						OR = {
							ai = yes
							has_country_flag = religious_news_major
						}
						OR = {
							is_defender_of_faith = yes
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
							papal_trigger = yes
							is_papal_controller = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = dg_catholic.080 days = 30 }
		}
		add_papal_influence = -10
		if = {
			limit = { advisor = theologian }
			random = { chance = 50 remove_advisor = theologian }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { advisor = inquisitor }
			random = { chance = 50 remove_advisor = inquisitor }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion = protestant
						religion = reformed
					}
					PAP = { NOT = { has_country_flag = first_reformation } }
				}
				PAP = { set_country_flag = first_reformation }
				AVI = { set_country_flag = first_reformation }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } }
				}
				subtract_stability_2 = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } }
				}
				subtract_stability_1 = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } }
				}
				subtract_stability_points_50 = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 4000 }
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 2000 }
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 1000 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 500 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 250 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 0 }
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				set_country_flag = excommunication_excommunicated
				country_event = { id = dg_pope.028 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #A warning from the pope
	
	id = dg_catholic.067
	title = dg_catholic.067.t
	desc = dg_catholic.067.d
	picture = catholic_excommunication
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #By dg_pope.027
	
	immediate = {
		add_country_modifier = { name = excommunication_reprieve duration = 3000 hidden = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_rome }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_rome
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_church }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_church
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_heathen_ally
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_blasphemy
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_papal_states
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_unjust_war
		}
		set_country_flag = excommunication_warning
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.066.b #Give back Rome

		random_ally = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }

				any_known_country = { war_with = PREV religion = catholic }
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = heathen_friendship_broken }
		}
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_rome
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_church
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy
		hidden_effect = {
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				set_country_flag = excommunication_repented
				country_event = { id = dg_pope.028 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.066.e #Leave the Papal States
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		trigger = { has_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { is_core = PAP NOT = { is_core = owner } }
			cede_province = PAP
		}
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_rome
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_church
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy
		hidden_effect = {
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				set_country_flag = excommunication_repented
				country_event = { id = dg_pope.028 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.067.a #Consider the implications
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_rome
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_church
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states
		clr_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war

			random_known_country = {
				limit = { is_papal_controller = yes }
				set_country_flag = excommunication_warned
				country_event = { id = dg_pope.028 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Excommunication (Breaking from Rome)
	
	id = dg_catholic.070
	title = dg_catholic.066.t
	desc = dg_catholic.070.d
	picture = catholic_excommunication
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = was_catholic
		NOT = { religion = catholic }
		PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 200 } }
		is_papal_controller = no
		is_excommunicated = no #Handled by separate event
		NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
		has_global_flag = living_pope
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 2 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = excommunicated }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = tolerant_hre }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_conversion
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = sheltered_luther }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_conversion
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { religion = catholic } has_country_flag = was_catholic }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_conversion
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_rome }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_rome
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_church }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_church
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_heathen_ally
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_blasphemy
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_papal_states
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = excommunication_unjust_war }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_us_unjust_war
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				OR = {
					war_with = ROOT
					alliance_with = ROOT
					truce_with = ROOT
					marriage_with = ROOT
					junior_union_with = ROOT
					senior_union_with = ROOT
					vassal_of = ROOT
					overlord_of = ROOT
					has_country_flag = religious_news_all
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
						is_neighbor_of = ROOT
					}
					AND = {
						religion = catholic
						OR = {
							is_defender_of_faith = yes
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
							papal_trigger = yes
							is_papal_controller = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = dg_catholic.080 days = 30 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.066.a #The church is against us
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_papal_influence = -10
		if = {
			limit = { advisor = theologian }
			random = { chance = 50 remove_advisor = theologian }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { advisor = inquisitor }
			random = { chance = 50 remove_advisor = inquisitor }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = protestant
					religion = reformed
				}
				PAP = { NOT = { has_country_flag = first_reformation } }
			}
			PAP = { set_country_flag = first_reformation }
			AVI = { set_country_flag = first_reformation }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } }
				}
				subtract_stability_3 = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } }
				}
				subtract_stability_2 = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } }
				}
				subtract_stability_1 = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 4000 }
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 2000 }
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 1000 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 500 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 250 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = repress_protestants_abroad
			clr_country_flag = counter_reformation
			clr_country_flag = catholic_reformation
			clr_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation
			clr_country_flag = reformation_maybe
			clr_country_flag = introduce_reformation
			clr_country_flag = spread_reformation
			clr_country_flag = refused_reformation
			clr_country_flag = renaissance
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Excommunication (Abuse of Papal Authority)
	
	id = dg_catholic.075
	title = dg_catholic.066.t
	desc = dg_catholic.075.d
	picture = catholic_excommunication
	
	trigger = {
		is_excommunicated = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }
		religion = catholic
		NOT = { has_country_flag = diplomatic_excommunication }
		is_papal_controller = no
		papal_trigger = no
		PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } }
		has_global_flag = living_pope
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 2 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = excommunicated }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				OR = {
					war_with = ROOT
					alliance_with = ROOT
					truce_with = ROOT
					marriage_with = ROOT
					junior_union_with = ROOT
					senior_union_with = ROOT
					vassal_of = ROOT
					overlord_of = ROOT
					has_country_flag = religious_news_all
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
						is_neighbor_of = ROOT
					}
					AND = {
						religion = catholic
						OR = {
							is_defender_of_faith = yes
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
							papal_trigger = yes
							is_papal_controller = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = dg_catholic.080 days = 30 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.066.a #The church is against us
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_papal_influence = -10
		set_country_flag = diplomatic_excommunication
		set_country_flag = unfair_excommunication
		if = {
			limit = { advisor = theologian }
			random = { chance = 50 remove_advisor = theologian }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { advisor = inquisitor }
			random = { chance = 50 remove_advisor = inquisitor }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } }
				}
				subtract_stability_3 = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } }
				}
				subtract_stability_2 = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } }
				}
				subtract_stability_1 = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 4000 }
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 2000 }
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 1000 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 500 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 250 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = repress_protestants_abroad

			clr_country_flag = introduce_reformation
			clr_country_flag = spread_reformation
			clr_country_flag = refused_reformation
			clr_country_flag = renaissance
		}

country_event = { #Consanguinity
	
	id = dg_catholic.076
	title = dg_catholic.076.t
	desc = dg_catholic.076.d
	picture = catholic_consanguinity
	
	trigger = {
		PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } }
		religion = catholic
		government = monarchy
		NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = consanguinity } }
		NOT = { PAP = { has_country_flag = limited_consanguinity_allowed } }
		is_subject_other_than_tributary_trigger = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = patronato_real }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = national_church }
		any_neighbor_country = {
			religion = catholic
			government = monarchy
			ai = yes
			NOT = { marriage_with = ROOT }
			NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
			is_subject_other_than_tributary_trigger = no
			OR = {
				culture_group = ROOT
				alliance_with = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { #Religious fervor does not apply here
		
		years = 416
		
		modifier = {
			num_of_royal_marriages = 1
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			num_of_royal_marriages = 2
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			num_of_royal_marriages = 3
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } } }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = consanguinity_problems
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = { set_country_flag = consanguinity }
			set_country_flag = consanguinity_issues
			set_country_flag = consanguinity_problems #Once this event happens to you, it will be less likely to happen again - game balance
			random_neighbor_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = catholic
					government = monarchy
					ai = yes
					NOT = { marriage_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					is_subject_other_than_tributary_trigger = no
					OR = {
						culture_group = ROOT
						alliance_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = engagement_on_hold
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation }
				}
				change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 }
			}
		} #End hidden effect
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.076.a #Ask the pope for dispensation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = ally_of_pope
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = friend_of_pope
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		add_papal_influence = -5
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = marriage_on_hold }
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.076.b #Break off the engagement
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				is_papal_controller = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_prestige = -5
		hidden_effect = { PAP = { clr_country_flag = consanguinity } }
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = engagement_on_hold }
			country_event = { id = dg_catholic.077 days = 30 }
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = engagement_broken }
			hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = engagement_on_hold }
		}
	}
}

		}

country_event = { #Dispensation Denied (consanguinity)
	
	id = dg_catholic.079
	title = dg_catholic.079.t
	desc = dg_catholic.079.d
	picture = catholic_papal_legate
	
	is_triggered_only = yes #By dg_pope.012
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = { clr_country_flag = consanguinity }
			PAP = { clr_country_flag = consanguinity_issues }
			set_country_flag = dispensation_was_denied
			clr_country_flag = marriage_on_hold
		}
		if = { #Invention of the printing press in 1450 allows for much faster and cheaper communication of problems
			limit = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = no }
			random = {
				chance = 25
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
						PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_simony value = 0.1 } }
					}
				}
				add_reform_desire = 0.001
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_casual_literacy_trigger = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = protestant } }
					PAP = { change_variable = { which = reform_desire_eccleistical_courts value = 0.1 } }
				}
			}
			add_reform_desire = 0.001
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation }
				}
				change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.079.a #Cover up our private shame
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = -2
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = PAP
						is_papal_controller = yes
					}
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = religious_scandal_pious }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = -1.5
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = PAP
						is_papal_controller = yes
					}
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = religious_scandal_observant }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = -1
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = PAP
						is_papal_controller = yes
					}
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = religious_scandal_decadent }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = -0.5
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = engagement_on_hold }
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = engagement_broken }
			hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = engagement_on_hold }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.079.b #Protest this rank injustice
		add_papal_influence = -5
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 100 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = PAP
						is_papal_controller = yes
					}
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = religious_scandal_fanatical }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_strong duration = 100 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = PAP
						is_papal_controller = yes
					}
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = religious_scandal_pious }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country duration = 100 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = PAP
						is_papal_controller = yes
					}
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = religious_scandal_observant }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = religious_scandal_country_weak duration = 100 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = PAP
						is_papal_controller = yes
					}
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = religious_scandal_decadent }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = neighbor_complaint
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = engagement_on_hold }
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = engagement_broken }
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = engagement_on_hold
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = renaissance
						NOT = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation }
					}
					change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #A nation is placed under interdict
	
	id = dg_catholic.080
	title = dg_catholic.080.t
	desc = dg_catholic.080.d
	picture = catholic_excommunication
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = tolerant_hre } }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_them_conversion

		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = sheltered_luther } }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_them_conversion
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { religion = catholic } has_country_flag = was_catholic } }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_them_conversion
			hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = excommunication_charges value = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = excommunication_rome } }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_them_rome
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = excommunication_church } }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_them_church
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = excommunication_heathen_ally } }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_them_heathen_ally
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy } }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_them_blasphemy
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = excommunication_papal_states } }
			custom_tooltip = excommunication_them_papal_states
		}
		if = {

			custom_tooltip = excommunication_them_unjust_war
		}
	}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = excommunicated }

				NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } } }
				factor = 0.85
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 350 } } }
				factor = 0.85
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } } }
				factor = 0.85
			}
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { religion = catholic }
				factor = 0.25
			}
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				government = theocracy
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				religion = catholic
				is_emperor = yes
				factor = 1.4
			}

			}

country_event = { #82 - The $MONARCHTITLE$'s Great Matter
	
	id = dg_catholic.082
	title = dg_catholic.082.t
	desc = dg_catholic.082.d
	picture = catholic_trial
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = annulment_refused
		NOT = { has_ruler_modifier = infertile_ruler }
		OR = {
			has_heir = no
			AND = {
				has_female_heir = yes
				heir_age = 2
			}
		}
		government = monarchy
		religion = catholic
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 2 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = annulment_granted
			clr_country_flag = annulment_refused
			clr_country_flag = annulment_process
			clr_country_flag = contested_annulment
			set_country_flag = great_matter
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = { has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation }
				}
				change_variable = { which = catholic_corruption value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_religion_enabled = protestant
					NOT = { has_country_flag = protestant_reaction }
					has_country_flag = renaissance
				}
				clr_country_flag = renaissance
				capital_scope = { clr_province_flag = renaissance_ideas }
			}
		}
		dg_reduce_legitimacy = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.082.a #Cover up our private shame
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = { legitimacy = 80 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { legitimacy = 60 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { legitimacy = 40 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { legitimacy = 20 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = marriage_broken } }
			country_event = { id = dg_catholic.088 days = 30 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.082.b #Go ahead with the divorce anyway
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		remove_country_modifier = loveless_marriage
		add_prestige = -5
		random = {
			chance = 30
			define_heir = { religion = catholic dynasty = ROOT }
			dg_add_legitimacy = yes
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = marriage_broken } }
			country_event = { id = dg_catholic.087 days = 30 }
		}
		country_event = { id = dg_catholic.061 }
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = great_matter
			set_country_flag = royal_scandal
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #86 - Annulment declared
	
	id = dg_catholic.086
	title = dg_catholic.086.t
	desc = dg_catholic.086.d
	picture = catholic_trial
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.086.a #This is a grave insult
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { num_of_cities = ROOT }
				}
				dg_reduce_legitimacy = yes
				dg_reduce_prestige_small = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { NOT = { num_of_cities = ROOT } }
				}
				dg_reduce_legitimacy_small = yes
				dg_reduce_prestige_small = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			dg_reduce_prestige_small = yes
		}
		add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = marriage_broken }
		FROM = {
			break_marriage = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_idea_group = diplomatic_ideas } }
					hidden_effect = { add_stability_1 = yes }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { dynasty = ROOT }
				PREV = { add_casus_belli = { target = FROM months = 120 type = cb_restore_personal_union } }
			}
			else = {
				PREV = { add_casus_belli = { target = FROM months = 120 type = cb_annulment } }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #91 - Rival Popes
	
	id = dg_catholic.091
	title = dg_catholic.091.t
	desc = dg_catholic.091.d
	picture = catholic_schism
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		exists = AVI
		exists = PAP
		AVI = { papal_trigger = yes }
		PAP = { papal_trigger = yes }
		papal_trigger = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = chosen_sides_in_schism }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 8
		
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = excommunication_sponsoring_schism
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.80
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			is_emperor = yes
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			is_defender_of_faith = yes
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			any_neighbor_country = { papal_trigger = yes }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			is_subject_other_than_tributary_trigger = yes
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = chosen_sides_in_schism
		add_papal_influence = -5
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
					}
				}
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.091.a #Support the Roman pope
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { #Initial enthusiasm
				NOT = { had_global_flag = { flag = catholic_schism days = 1000 } }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				any_neighbor_country = { tag = PAP }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { culture_group = ROOT }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { primary_culture = ROOT }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				is_rival = PAP
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_enemy = PAP
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				war_with = PAP
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				truce_with = PAP
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				alliance_with = PAP
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				dynasty = PAP
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				any_rival_country = { has_country_flag = support_antipope }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				any_enemy_country = { has_country_flag = support_antipope }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				any_ally = { has_country_flag = support_roman_pope }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				any_known_country = { culture_group = ROOT has_country_flag = support_roman_pope }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				any_rival_country = { has_country_flag = support_roman_pope }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				any_enemy_country = { has_country_flag = support_roman_pope }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				any_ally = { has_country_flag = support_antipope }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				any_known_country = { culture_group = ROOT has_country_flag = support_antipope }
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				any_neighbor_country = { tag = AVI }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				AVI = { culture_group = ROOT }
				factor = 0.5
