			modifier = {
				AVI = { primary_culture = ROOT }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_rival = AVI
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				is_enemy = AVI
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				war_with = AVI
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				truce_with = AVI
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				alliance_with = AVI
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				dynasty = AVI
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				overlord = { has_country_flag = support_roman_pope }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				overlord = { has_country_flag = support_antipope }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { has_country_flag = regular_councils_promised }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				PAP = { check_variable = { which = council_topic_schism value = 1 } }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = excommunicated
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = support_roman_pope
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = support_antipope
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = support_roman_pope
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = support_antipope }
			clr_country_flag = support_antipope
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -8
				add_legitimacy = -4
				add_papal_influence = 16
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -6
				add_legitimacy = -3
				add_papal_influence = 12
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -4
				add_legitimacy = -2
				add_papal_influence = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -2
				add_legitimacy = -1
				add_papal_influence = 4
			}
		}
		AVI = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					papal_trigger = yes
					religion = catholic
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = support_antipope
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { tag = AVI }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				AVI = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							papal_trigger = yes
							religion = catholic
							NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						}
						add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = support_antipope
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { tag = AVI }
					}
					reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = support_antipope
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { tag = AVI }
					}
					reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = support_antipope
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { tag = AVI }
					}
					reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = support_antipope
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { tag = AVI }
					}
					reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.091.b #Support the Antipope
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		set_country_flag = support_antipope
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = support_roman_pope }
			clr_country_flag = support_roman_pope
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = -8
				add_legitimacy = -4
				add_papal_influence = 16
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = -6
				add_legitimacy = -3
				add_papal_influence = 12
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = -4
				add_legitimacy = -2
				add_papal_influence = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = -2
				add_legitimacy = -1
				add_papal_influence = 4
			}
		}
		PAP = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					papal_trigger = yes
					religion = catholic
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = support_roman_pope
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { tag = PAP }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				AVI = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							papal_trigger = yes
							religion = catholic
							NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						}
						add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = support_roman_pope
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { tag = PAP }
					}
					reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = support_roman_pope
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { tag = PAP }
					}
					reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = support_roman_pope
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { tag = PAP }
					}
					reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = support_roman_pope
						religion = catholic
						NOT = { tag = PAP }
					}
					reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Schism notifier
	
	id = dg_catholic.092
	title = dg_catholic.092.t
	desc = dg_catholic.092.d
	picture = catholic_schism
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.092.a
	}
}

country_event = { #End of the Schism
	
	id = dg_catholic.093
	title = dg_catholic.093.t
	desc = dg_catholic.093.d
	picture = catholic_return_to_rome
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		NOT = { AVI = { num_of_cities = 1 papal_trigger = yes } }
		any_known_country = {
			OR = {
				has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
				has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
				has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
				has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 1 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = supported_antipope
			clr_country_flag = supported_roman_pope
			clr_country_flag = excommunication_sponsoring_schism
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
						has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
					}
				}
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_fanatical }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_pious }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_observant }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = rival_popes_decadent }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.093.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = antipope_wins
					has_country_flag = supported_antipope
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = antipope_wins }
					has_country_flag = supported_roman_pope
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.60 }
			add_prestige = 4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = 0.20 }
			add_prestige = 3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.20 }
			add_prestige = 2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { piety = -0.60 }
			add_prestige = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.093.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = antipope_wins
						has_country_flag = supported_antipope
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = antipope_wins }
						has_country_flag = supported_roman_pope
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #94 - The Archbishop of $COUNTRY$
	
	id = dg_catholic.094
	title = dg_catholic.094.t
	desc = dg_catholic.094.d
	picture = catholic_order_founded
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		NOT = { government = theocracy }
		patriarch_authority = 0.10
		is_papal_controller = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = national_church }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = patronato_real }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarchate_vacant }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { years = 16 }
	
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = clerical_advisor
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_appointed
			#The pope may choose a religious head especially for you if he cares
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
						has_country_modifier = protestant_sympathies
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } } }
					random = { chance = 50 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } } }
					random = { chance = 40 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } } }
					random = { chance = 30 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 200 } } }
					random = { chance = 20 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 100 } } }
					random = { chance = 10 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = protestant_sympathies }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } } }
					random = { chance = 25 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } } }
					random = { chance = 20 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } } }
					random = { chance = 15 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 200 } } }
					random = { chance = 10 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 100 } } }
					random = { chance = 5 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
			}
			#The pope decides what a country best needs
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { religious_unity = 1.00 } }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_theologian value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { religious_unity = 0.90 } }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_theologian value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { religious_unity = 0.80 } }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_theologian value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { religious_unity = 0.70 } }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_theologian value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = 0 } }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_obedient value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { stability = -2 } }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_obedient value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1 }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_obedient value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { religious_unity = 1.00 }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_obedient value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_at_war = yes }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_zealous value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { at_war_with_religious_enemy = yes }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_zealous value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { war_score = 0 } }
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_zealous value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { num_of_missionaries = 1 }
					NOT = { religious_unity = 1.00 }
				}
				change_variable = { which = patriarch_zealous value = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = patriarch_zealous value = 1 }
					check_variable = { which = patriarch_zealous which = patriarch_obedient }
					check_variable = { which = patriarch_zealous which = patriarch_theologian }
				}
				set_country_flag = patriarch_aim_zealous
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = patriarch_theologian value = 1 }
					check_variable = { which = patriarch_theologian which = patriarch_obedient }
					check_variable = { which = patriarch_theologian which = patriarch_zealous }
				}
				set_country_flag = patriarch_aim_theologian
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = patriarch_obedient value = 1 }
					check_variable = { which = patriarch_obedient which = patriarch_theologian }
					check_variable = { which = patriarch_obedient which = patriarch_zealous }
				}
				set_country_flag = patriarch_aim_obedient
			}
			set_variable = { which = patriarch_obedient value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = patriarch_theologian value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = patriarch_zealous value = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ally_of_pope }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = patriarch_aim_obedient }
					random = { chance = 50 set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = patriarch_aim_zealous }
					random = { chance = 50 set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = patriarch_aim_theologian }
					random = { chance = 50 set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = friend_of_pope }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = patriarch_aim_obedient }
					random = { chance = 25 set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = patriarch_aim_zealous }
					random = { chance = 25 set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = patriarch_aim_theologian }
					random = { chance = 25 set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian }
				}
			}
			#Corrupt popes may assign corrupt heads
			if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { has_country_flag = corrupt_pope }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_zealous }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } } }
					random = { chance = 25 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } } }
					random = { chance = 20 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } } }
					random = { chance = 15 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 200 } } }
					random = { chance = 10 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 100 } } }
					random = { chance = 5 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = { has_country_flag = secular_pope }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_zealous }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 500 } } }
					random = { chance = 10 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 400 } } }
					random = { chance = 8 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 300 } } }
					random = { chance = 6 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 200 } } }
					random = { chance = 4 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { PAP = { check_variable = { which = papal_authority value = 100 } } }
					random = { chance = 2 set_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
				}
			}
			#If no special head is selected, a random head will be chosen
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_theologian }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_zealous }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt }
				}
				random_list = {
					25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_theologian }
					25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_zealous }
					25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_obedient }
					25 = { set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial }
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_aim_zealous
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_aim_theologian
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_aim_obedient
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope }
			custom_tooltip = new_archbishop_enemy
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = rival_of_pope }
			custom_tooltip = new_archbishop_rival
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = friend_of_pope }
			custom_tooltip = new_archbishop_friend
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ally_of_pope }
			custom_tooltip = new_archbishop_ally
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = new_archbishop_random
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.094.a #Welcome him to $CAPITAL_CITY$
	}
	after = {
		dg_patriarch_triggers = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #141 - Jesuit Mission
	
	id = dg_catholic.141
	title = dg_catholic.141.t
	desc = dg_catholic.141.d
	picture = catholic_jesuit_mission
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_proposed }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = jesuits_suppressed }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = jesuits_expelled }
		any_known_country = {
			NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
			NOT = { religion_group = jewish_group }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = theology }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 41
		
		modifier = {
			PAP = { has_country_flag = jesuits_limited }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.20 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { piety = -0.60 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.75
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = { patriarch_authority = 0.25 }
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			num_of_colonies = 1
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			colony = 1
			factor = 0.5
		}
		#	modifier = {
		#		trade_company_size = 1
		#		factor = 0.5
		#		}
		modifier = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
				NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
				NOT = { religion_group = jewish_group }
			}
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_country_flag = jesuit_missions_proposed }
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.141.a #Build a college
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		set_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
		set_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
		if = { #Maximum
			limit = { monthly_income = 200 }
			add_treasury = -200
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { monthly_income = 4 }
			add_years_of_income = -0.08
		}
		else = { #Minimum
			add_treasury = -4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 2 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 4 } }
			}
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.75 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = theology duration = 2000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.50 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = theology duration = 1000 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.25 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = theology duration = 500 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = theology duration = 250 }
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { continent = europe }
				NOT = { base_tax = 6 }
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = {
						NOT = { religion_group = christian }
						NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
						NOT = { religion_group = jewish_group }
					}
				}
				university_province_trigger = no
				num_free_building_slots = 1
			}
			add_building = small_university
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.141.b #Allow them in our colonies
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		set_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.141.c #Forbid them from interfering
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.80 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_powerful duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.60 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_strong duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.40 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_moderate duration = 500 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.20 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_weak duration = 500 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = unhappy_church_impotent duration = 500 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #142 - Governor allows missionaries into $PROVINCENAME$
	
	id = dg_catholic.142
	title = dg_catholic.142.t
	desc = dg_catholic.142.d
	picture = catholic_jesuits_asia
	
	trigger = {
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				asia_continent_trigger = yes
				africa_continent_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		num_of_cities = 20
		NOT = { has_country_flag = black_robes_arrived }
		any_known_country = {
			has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
			religion = catholic
			check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
			NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
		}
		NOT = { religion_group = christian }
		NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
		NOT = { religion_group = jewish_group }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 41
		
		modifier = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
				religion = catholic
				check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
				religion = catholic
				check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = black_robes_arrived
		#Selects province
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owner = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = event_target } } }
					is_capital = no
					has_port = yes
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							religion = catholic
							has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
							has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
							check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
							NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = event_target
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owner = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = event_target } } }
					is_capital = no
					has_port = yes
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							religion = catholic
							has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
							check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
							NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = event_target
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owner = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = event_target } } }
					is_capital = no
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							religion = catholic
							has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
							has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
							check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = event_target
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owner = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = event_target } } }
					is_capital = no
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							religion = catholic
							has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
							check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = event_target
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owner = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = event_target } } }
					is_capital = no
					has_port = yes
					NOT = { any_neighbor_province = { is_capital = yes } }
				}
				set_province_flag = event_target
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owner = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = event_target } } }
					is_capital = no
					has_port = yes
				}
				set_province_flag = event_target
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { owner = { any_owned_province = { has_province_flag = event_target } } }
					is_capital = no
				}
				set_province_flag = event_target
			}
			if = {
				limit = { num_of_cities = 30 }
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							area = PREV
						}
						set_province_flag = event_target
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { num_of_cities = 90 }
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							region = PREV
						}
						set_province_flag = event_target
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.142.a #Observe this situation quietly
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		set_country_flag = jesuits_tolerated
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
			clr_province_flag = event_target
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
			}
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_strong }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 10
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = sympathetic_ruler_fanatical }
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported }
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_weak }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 5
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = sympathetic_ruler_pious }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.142.b #Summon them to $CAPITAL_CITY$
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = christians_banned
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = chinese_rites_banned
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		add_adm_power = -10
		set_country_flag = jesuits_tolerated
		set_country_flag = jesuits_summoned
		country_event = { id = dg_catholic.143 days = 90 }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
			clr_province_flag = event_target
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.142.c #Replace the governor
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = christians_permitted
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = christians_tolerated
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = christians_banned
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = chinese_rites_banned
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = { #They can see first hand the divisions within Christianity
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = chaldean value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = protestant value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = coptic value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = orthodox value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = reformed value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = gnostic value = 2 }
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		add_adm_power = -50
		random = {
			chance = 50
			subtract_stability_1 = yes
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = event_target }
			clr_province_flag = event_target
			custom_tooltip = minority_grows_5
			hidden_effect = {
				random = {
					chance = 50
					change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
					change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Black Robes visit $CAPITAL_CITY$
	
	id = dg_catholic.143
	title = dg_catholic.143.t
	desc = dg_catholic.143.d
	picture = catholic_jesuits_asia
	
	trigger = {
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				asia_continent_trigger = yes
				africa_continent_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { num_of_cities = 20 }
			has_country_flag = jesuits_summoned
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = black_robes_arrived }
			has_country_flag = jesuits_summoned
		}
		any_known_country = {
			has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
			religion = catholic
			check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
		}
		NOT = { religion_group = christian }
		NOT = { religion_group = muslim }
		NOT = { religion_group = jewish_group }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		years = 41
		
		modifier = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
				religion = catholic
				check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
				religion = catholic
				check_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 }
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier }
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = jesuits_summoned
		set_country_flag = black_robes_arrived
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = chaldean value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = protestant value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = coptic value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = orthodox value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = reformed value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = gnostic value = 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = local_christian_sects_persecuted
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.143.a #Allow them to remain in $CAPITAL_CITY$
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		set_country_flag = jesuit_missions_allowed
		add_adm_power = 100
		add_dip_power = 50
		define_advisor = { religion = catholic type = natural_scientist discount = yes }
		define_advisor = { religion = catholic type = theologian discount = yes }
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_tolerance duration = 2000 }
		add_piety = -0.20
		capital_scope = {
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = { num_of_cities = 30 }
					NOT = { owner = { num_of_cities = 90 } }
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						area = PREV
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
						change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { num_of_cities = 90 } }
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						region = PREV
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
						change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = minority_usefulness value = 30 }
			set_country_flag = useful_catholic
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_strong }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 10
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = sympathetic_ruler_fanatical }
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported }
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_weak }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 5
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = sympathetic_ruler_pious }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.143.b #Limit them to the hinterlands
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		trigger = {
			num_of_cities = 4
			any_owned_province = {
				#Only territories
				NOT = { base_tax = 5 }
				OR = {
					any_neighbor_province = { NOT = { base_tax = 5 } }
					has_owner_accepted_culture = no
				}
				is_capital = no
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = jesuit_missions_allowed
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				#Only territories
				NOT = { base_tax = 5 }
				OR = {
					any_neighbor_province = { NOT = { base_tax = 5 } }
					has_owner_accepted_culture = no
				}
				is_capital = no
			}
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
			}
			#Change to area if 30+ and region if 90+
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = minority_usefulness value = 30 }
			set_country_flag = useful_catholic
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_weak }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 5
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = sympathetic_ruler_pious }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.143.c #Limit them to the trade cities
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		trigger = {
			num_of_cities = 4
			any_owned_province = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier
					AND = {
						base_tax = 7
						has_port = yes
					}
				}
				is_capital = no
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = jesuit_missions_allowed
		add_dip_power = 100
		random_list = {
			50 = { define_advisor = { religion = catholic type = trader discount = yes } }
			50 = { define_advisor = { religion = catholic type = navigator discount = yes } }
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier
					AND = {
						has_port = yes
						base_tax = 7
					}
				}
				is_capital = no
			}
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = minority_usefulness value = 30 }
			set_country_flag = useful_catholic
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_weak }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 20
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = sympathetic_ruler_pious }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.143.e #Ban them from $COUNTRY$
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = chaldean value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = protestant value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = coptic value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = orthodox value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = reformed value = 2 }
						check_variable = { which = gnostic value = 2 }
					}
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		add_adm_power = -50
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 2000 }
		add_piety = 0.20
	}
}

country_event = { #Jesuit Missionaries
	
	id = dg_catholic.144
	title = dg_catholic.144.t
	desc = dg_catholic.144.d
	picture = catholic_monks_preaching
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_allowed
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = christians_banned }
		NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = heretic_missionary } }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 50 }
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = jesuit_missions_allowed
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.144.a #Let them continue
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
			add_province_modifier = { name = heretic_missionary duration = 500 }
			hidden_effect = {
				random = {
					chance = 50
					change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
					change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = minority_usefulness value = 30 }
			set_country_flag = useful_catholic
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_strong }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 10
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = sympathetic_ruler_fanatical }
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported }
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_weak }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 5
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = sympathetic_ruler_pious }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.144.b #Place limits on their work
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		add_adm_power = -25
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 2000 }
		add_piety = 0.20
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
			custom_tooltip = minority_grows_5
			hidden_effect = {
				random = {
					chance = 50
					change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
					change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.144.c #Grant them our protection
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		add_adm_power = -25
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_tolerance duration = 4000 }
		add_piety = -0.20
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
			}
			random_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
					owned_by = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
					change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = minority_usefulness value = 60 }
			set_country_flag = useful_catholic
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_strong }
				hidden_effect = {
					random_active_trade_node = {
						limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
						add_trade_modifier = {
							who = PREV
							duration = 4000
							power = 10
							key = minority_contacts
						}
					}
				}
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = sympathetic_ruler_fanatical }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
				}
				reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_weak }
				hidden_effect = {
					random_active_trade_node = {
						limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
						add_trade_modifier = {
							who = PREV
							duration = 4000
							power = 5
							key = minority_contacts
						}
					}
				}
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = sympathetic_ruler_pious }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.144.e #Embrace this foreign faith
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 4 } }
			is_force_converted = no
		}
		add_adm_power = -100
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
			}
			random_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
					owned_by = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
					change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = voluntary_conversion
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_religion_enabled = catholic } }
			custom_tooltip = convert_dangerous_religion
			subtract_stability_1 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = catholic_population value = 75 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_population_75
			add_stability_1 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = catholic_population value = 50 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_population_50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = catholic_population value = 25 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_population_25
			subtract_stability_1 = yes
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = convert_population_0
			subtract_stability_2 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.75 }
			custom_tooltip = convert_church_strong
			subtract_stability_2 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.50 }
			custom_tooltip = convert_piety_moderate
			subtract_stability_1 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { patriarch_authority = 0.25 }
			custom_tooltip = convert_church_weak
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = convert_church_insignificant
		}
		if = {
			limit = { advisor = theologian }
			custom_tooltip = convert_theologian
			add_stability_1 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = { religion = catholic }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ADM = 5
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_strong
				add_stability_3 = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ADM = 3
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_moderate
				add_stability_2 = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_weak
				add_stability_1 = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ADM = 5
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_moderate
				add_stability_2 = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ADM = 3
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_weak
				add_stability_1 = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_incompetent
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = was_catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { which = sympathy_to_old_religion value = 1 }
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_previous_recent
				add_stability_2 = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = convert_previous_old
				add_stability_1 = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = was_catholic }
				check_variable = { which = sympathy_to_old_religion value = 1 }
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_recent
			add_stability_1 = yes
		}
		change_religion = catholic
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = { which = jesuit_support value = 1 } }
	}
}

country_event = { #Fanatical Christians
	
	id = dg_catholic.145
	title = dg_catholic.145.t
	desc = dg_catholic.145.d
	picture = catholic_burning_church
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = black_robes_arrived
		NOT = { has_country_flag = fransiscans_arrived }
		NOT = { religion = catholic }
		any_owned_province = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 4 } }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { years = 20 }
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = fransiscans_arrived
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance }
			remove_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
			add_piety = 0.20
		}
		hidden_effect = { PAP = { set_country_flag = chinese_rites_debated } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.145.b #Expel the foreign devils
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 4000 }
		add_piety = 0.20
		clr_country_flag = useful_catholic
		add_adm_power = -50
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 10 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 500 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 8 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 400 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 6 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 300 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 4 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 200 }
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.145.a #Turn a blind eye to the persecution
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = religious_intolerance duration = 2000 }
		add_piety = 0.20

		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 10 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 500 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 8 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 400 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 6 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 300 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 4 } }
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 200 }
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.145.c #Step in to protect the Christians
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { which = minority_usefulness value = 60 }
			set_country_flag = useful_catholic
		}
		set_country_flag = jesuit_missions_allowed
		subtract_stability_1 = yes
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_owner_religion = yes
				check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = religious_riots duration = 500 }
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
				change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
			}
			random_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
					owned_by = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 }
					change_variable = { which = province_religion value = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_strong }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 10
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = aided_coreligionists_fanatical }
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = { has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported }
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = missionary_sponsor_weak }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = { strongest_trade_power = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 5
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = aided_coreligionists_pious }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #$PRIMARY_CULTURE$ Christianity
	
	id = dg_catholic.146
	title = dg_catholic.146.t
	desc = dg_catholic.146.d
	picture = catholic_jesuits_asia
	
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		has_country_flag = black_robes_arrived
		NOT = { has_country_flag = true_catholic }
		NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
		is_colonial_nation = no
		is_former_colonial_nation = no
		is_force_converted = no
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { years = 8 }
	
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.146.a #Stay true to the pope
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		set_country_flag = true_catholic
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.146.b #Our faith must adapt to our culture
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		subtract_stability_1 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { asia_continent_trigger = yes } }
			change_religion = chaldean
			force_converted = yes
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
				change_variable = { which = chaldean which = catholic }
				set_variable = { which = catholic value = 0 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { africa_continent_trigger = yes } }
			change_religion = coptic
			force_converted = yes
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
				change_variable = { which = coptic which = catholic }
				set_variable = { which = catholic value = 0 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			change_religion = gnostic
			force_converted = yes
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = catholic value = 2 } }
				change_variable = { which = gnostic which = catholic }
				set_variable = { which = catholic value = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #161 - Patriarchal Reunion
	
	id = dg_catholic.161
	title = dg_catholic.161.t
	desc = dg_catholic.161.d
	picture = catholic_bishop
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate
		NOT = { has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy }
		owner = {
			religion = catholic
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				has_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate
				NOT = { has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy }
				culture_group = ROOT
				value = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		
		months = 25
		
		modifier = {
			is_capital = yes
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	
	#immediate = {
	#	set_province_flag = rival_latin_patriarch
	#}
	
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.161.a #Move it to here
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		owner = {
			add_papal_influence = 100
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = 10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = 2
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate
					NOT = { has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy }
					culture_group = ROOT
				}
				clr_province_flag = catholic_patriarchate
				set_province_flag = catholic_archbishopric
				remove_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate
				add_province_modifier = { name = catholic_archbishopric duration = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.161.b #Close here down
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				is_capital = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_owner_culture = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_papal_influence = 100
			if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.60 }
				add_prestige = 10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = 0.20 }
				add_prestige = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.20 }
				add_prestige = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { piety = -0.60 }
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = 2
			}
		}
		clr_province_flag = catholic_patriarchate
		set_province_flag = catholic_archbishopric
		remove_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate
		add_province_modifier = { name = catholic_archbishopric duration = -1 }
	}
}
